A p p l i c a t i o n \ B a c k t e s t i n g \ B a c k t e s t S n a p s h o t s . c s T Y P E : . c s S I Z E : 1 . 6 4 K B L I N E S : 4 4 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = namespace TQGA.Application.Backtesting; /// /// Immutable snapshot of per-strategy trading diagnostics, /// copied out of the DI-scoped TradeDecisionDiagnostics service. /// public sealed class TradeDecisionDiagnosticsSnapshot { public int TicksProcessed { get; init; } public int SignalLong { get; init; } public int SignalShort { get; init; } public int SignalExit { get; init; } public int EntryAttempts { get; init; } public int ExecutedEntries { get; init; } public int ExecutedExits { get; init; } } /// /// Chronological train/test fold result for true walk-forward validation. /// public sealed class WalkForwardFoldSnapshot { public int FoldNo { get; init; } public DateTime TrainStartUtc { get; init; } public DateTime TrainEndUtc { get; init; } public DateTime TestStartUtc { get; init; } public DateTime TestEndUtc { get; init; } public decimal StartEquity { get; init; } public decimal EndEquity { get; init; } public decimal ReturnPct { get; init; } public int TestPoints { get; init; } } /// /// Lightweight strategy fitness DTO used by A84 reporting layer. /// public sealed class StrategyFitnessSnapshot { public int StrategyId { get; init; } public string StrategyCode { get; init; } = string.Empty; public decimal PnL { get; init; } public int Trades { get; init; } public int Exits { get; init; } public decimal FitnessScore { get; init; } public bool Allowed { get; init; } public string GateReason { get; init; } = string.Empty; } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ B a c k t e s t i n g \ P o r t f o l i o B a c k t e s t R e s u l t . c s T Y P E : . c s S I Z E : 1 . 7 5 K B L I N E S : 2 5 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = using System; using System.Collections.Generic; namespace TQGA.Application.Backtesting; public sealed class PortfolioBacktestResult { public Dictionary StrategyPnL { get; set; } = new(); public Dictionary SymbolPnL { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); public Dictionary CapitalWeights { get; set; } = new(); public Dictionary PortfolioEquityTimeline { get; set; } = new(); public Dictionary SymbolTimeframePnL { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); public Dictionary StrategySymbolTimeframePnL { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); public Dictionary StrategyDiagnostics { get; set; } = new(); public Dictionary MarketSelectionRejections { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); public List SelectedMarkets { get; set; } = new(); public List WalkForwardFolds { get; set; } = new(); // Runner-layer raw CIO / market allocation public Dictionary CioSymbolTimeframeWeights { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); public Dictionary MarketAllocationWeights { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); public decimal CashAllocationWeight { get; set; } // PATCH 3: canonical post-gating CIO state used by all downstream reports public Dictionary CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights { get; set; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); public bool HasMarketAllocationWeights => MarketAllocationWeights != null && MarketAllocationWeights.Count > 0; } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ B a c k t e s t i n g \ P o r t f o l i o B a c k t e s t R u n n e r . c s T Y P E : . c s S I Z E : 4 2 . 1 4 K B L I N E S : 9 6 5 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection; using TQGA.Application.Accounting; using TQGA.Application.Interfaces; using TQGA.Application.Portfolio; using TQGA.Application.Risk; using TQGA.Application.Strategy; using TQGA.Application.Trading; using TQGA.Domain.Market; namespace TQGA.Application.Backtesting; public sealed class PortfolioBacktestRunner { private readonly IServiceProvider _root; private readonly StrategyFactory _factory; private readonly ICandleDataFeed _feed; private const decimal PortfolioCapital = 100_000m; // WAVE B â€” institutional scarcity controls private const int WaveBTopNMarkets = 8; private const int WaveBMinMarkets = 5; private const int WaveBPerSymbolCap = 1; private const decimal WaveBMinScoreThreshold = 0.55m; private const decimal WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket = 0.20m; public PortfolioBacktestRunner( IServiceProvider root, StrategyFactory factory, ICandleDataFeed feed) { _root = root; _factory = factory; _feed = feed; } public Task RunAsync( IEnumerable strategyTypes, CancellationToken ct) { return RunAsync( strategyTypes, BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols, BinanceUniverse.Timeframes, FrictionProfile.Default, ct); } public Task RunAsync( IEnumerable strategyTypes, IReadOnlyList selectedTimeframes, FrictionProfile friction, CancellationToken ct) { return RunAsync( strategyTypes, BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols, selectedTimeframes, friction, ct); } public async Task RunAsync( IEnumerable strategyTypes, IReadOnlyList selectedSymbols, IReadOnlyList selectedTimeframes, FrictionProfile friction, CancellationToken ct) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(strategyTypes); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedSymbols); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedTimeframes); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(friction); var types = strategyTypes.ToList(); if (types.Count == 0) throw new InvalidOperationException("No strategies registered."); var activeSymbols = selectedSymbols.Count == 0 ? BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols.ToList() : selectedSymbols .Where(x => BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols.Contains(x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) .ToList(); if (activeSymbols.Count == 0) throw new InvalidOperationException("No valid symbols selected."); var activeTimeframes = selectedTimeframes.Count == 0 ? BinanceUniverse.Timeframes.ToList() : selectedTimeframes .Where(x => BinanceUniverse.Timeframes.Contains(x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) .ToList(); if (activeTimeframes.Count == 0) throw new InvalidOperationException("No valid timeframes selected."); var selection = new PreTradeMarketSelectionService() .SelectMarkets( _feed, activeSymbols, activeTimeframes, topN: 12); var rankedSelectedMarkets = selection.SelectedMarkets.ToList(); if (rankedSelectedMarkets.Count == 0) throw new InvalidOperationException("No markets passed pre-trade selection."); var combinedRejections = new Dictionary( selection.RejectedMarkets, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); var waveBSelection = ApplyWaveBSelection(rankedSelectedMarkets, combinedRejections); var selectedMarkets = waveBSelection.SelectedMarkets; if (selectedMarkets.Count == 0) throw new InvalidOperationException("No markets passed Wave B signal ranking and Top-N execution."); var marketAllocationWeights = waveBSelection.AllocationWeights; var unallocatedCashWeight = waveBSelection.CashWeight; var leadershipRank = new Dictionary(); for (int i = 0; i < selectedMarkets.Count; i++) leadershipRank[selectedMarkets[i]] = i + 1; var riskBudget = new PortfolioRiskBudgetEngine(); var rawNetPnlByMarket = selectedMarkets.ToDictionary(m => m, _ => 0m); var tradeCountByMarket = selectedMarkets.ToDictionary(m => m, _ => 0); var positiveStrategyHitsByMarket = selectedMarkets.ToDictionary(m => m, _ => 0); var strategyParticipationByMarket = selectedMarkets.ToDictionary(m => m, _ => 0); var nodes = new List(); var capitalWeights = new Dictionary(); // ECONOMIC TRUTH LAYER var symbolTfPnL = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); var strategySymbolTfPnL = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); var strategyDiagnostics = new Dictionary(); var adjustedPnlTimeline = new SortedDictionary(); // Institutional trust-weighted capital map var trustWeightsByType = BuildStrategyTrustWeights(types); int id = 1; foreach (var type in types) { using var scope = _root.CreateScope(); var strategy = _factory.Create(type); var engine = ActivatorUtilities.CreateInstance( scope.ServiceProvider, strategy); var ledger = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService(); var equity = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService(); var capital = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService(); var diag = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService(); decimal strategyWeight = trustWeightsByType.TryGetValue(type, out var resolvedWeight) ? resolvedWeight : 0m; capital.Seed(PortfolioCapital, strategyWeight); decimal allocatedCapital = PortfolioCapital * strategyWeight; equity.Seed(allocatedCapital); capitalWeights[id] = strategyWeight; if (strategyWeight <= 0m) { strategyDiagnostics[id] = new TradeDecisionDiagnosticsSnapshot { TicksProcessed = 0, SignalLong = 0, SignalShort = 0, SignalExit = 0, EntryAttempts = 0, ExecutedEntries = 0, ExecutedExits = 0 }; nodes.Add(new StrategyBacktestNode( id, strategy.Name, ledger, equity)); id++; continue; } var openRiskBySymbol = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); var openRiskByCluster = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); decimal totalOpenRiskPct = 0m; decimal peakEquity = allocatedCapital; foreach (var m in selectedMarkets) { var marketWeight = marketAllocationWeights.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedMarketWeight) ? resolvedMarketWeight : 0m; if (marketWeight <= 0m) continue; var candles = _feed.GetCandles(m.Symbol, m.Timeframe) .OrderBy(c => c.Time) .ToList(); if (candles.Count < 120) continue; var currentEquity = System.Math.Max(1m, allocatedCapital + ledger.TotalPnL); peakEquity = System.Math.Max(peakEquity, currentEquity); var drawdownPct = peakEquity <= 0m ? 0m : ((peakEquity - currentEquity) / peakEquity) * 100m; var budget = riskBudget.Evaluate( m.Symbol, m.Timeframe, candles, currentEquity, drawdownPct, openRiskBySymbol, openRiskByCluster, totalOpenRiskPct); if (!budget.IsAllowed) continue; openRiskBySymbol[m.Symbol] = (openRiskBySymbol.TryGetValue(m.Symbol, out var sRisk) ? sRisk : 0m) + budget.AllowedRiskPct; var cluster = budget.Cluster; openRiskByCluster[cluster] = (openRiskByCluster.TryGetValue(cluster, out var cRisk) ? cRisk : 0m) + budget.AllowedRiskPct; totalOpenRiskPct += budget.AllowedRiskPct; var beforePnl = GetSymbolPnL(ledger, m.Symbol); var beforeTradeCount = GetTradeCount(ledger); foreach (var candle in candles) { await engine.OnTickAsync( m.Symbol, candle.Close, candle.Time, ct); } var afterPnl = GetSymbolPnL(ledger, m.Symbol); var afterTradeCount = GetTradeCount(ledger); var newlyClosedTrades = ledger.Trades .Skip(beforeTradeCount) .Where(t => t.IsClosed) .ToList(); var grossDelta = afterPnl - beforePnl; var marketTradeCount = System.Math.Max(0, afterTradeCount - beforeTradeCount); var budgetScale = budget.AllowedRiskPct <= 0m ? 0m : budget.AllowedRiskPct / 0.50m; var effectiveScale = budgetScale * marketWeight; var scaledGrossDelta = grossDelta * effectiveScale; var frictionCost = EstimateFrictionCost( budget.PositionValue * marketWeight, marketTradeCount, friction, candles); var netDelta = scaledGrossDelta - frictionCost; AllocateNetDeltaAcrossClosedTrades( newlyClosedTrades, netDelta, candles[^1].Time, adjustedPnlTimeline); var keyTf = $"{m.Symbol}::{m.Timeframe}"; if (symbolTfPnL.ContainsKey(keyTf)) symbolTfPnL[keyTf] += netDelta; else symbolTfPnL[keyTf] = netDelta; var keyStrTf = $"S{id:00}::{m.Symbol}::{m.Timeframe}"; if (strategySymbolTfPnL.ContainsKey(keyStrTf)) strategySymbolTfPnL[keyStrTf] += netDelta; else strategySymbolTfPnL[keyStrTf] = netDelta; rawNetPnlByMarket[m] += netDelta; tradeCountByMarket[m] += marketTradeCount; strategyParticipationByMarket[m] += 1; if (netDelta > 0m) positiveStrategyHitsByMarket[m] += 1; openRiskBySymbol[m.Symbol] = System.Math.Max(0m, openRiskBySymbol[m.Symbol] - budget.AllowedRiskPct); openRiskByCluster[cluster] = System.Math.Max(0m, openRiskByCluster[cluster] - budget.AllowedRiskPct); totalOpenRiskPct = System.Math.Max(0m, totalOpenRiskPct - budget.AllowedRiskPct); } strategyDiagnostics[id] = new TradeDecisionDiagnosticsSnapshot { TicksProcessed = diag.TicksProcessed, SignalLong = diag.SignalLong, SignalShort = diag.SignalShort, SignalExit = diag.SignalExit, EntryAttempts = diag.EntryAttempts, ExecutedEntries = diag.ExecutedEntries, ExecutedExits = diag.ExecutedExits }; nodes.Add(new StrategyBacktestNode( id, strategy.Name, ledger, equity)); id++; } var compositeMarketScore = BuildCompositeMarketScores( selectedMarkets, rawNetPnlByMarket, tradeCountByMarket, positiveStrategyHitsByMarket, strategyParticipationByMarket, leadershipRank); var cio = new CioDynamicReallocationEngine( topK: 6, minWeight: 0.00m, maxWeight: 0.35m, maxWeightPerSymbol: 0.45m); var cioWeights = cio.ComputeWeights(compositeMarketScore); var adjustedSymbolPnL = AggregateAdjustedSymbolPnL(symbolTfPnL); var adjustedStrategyPnL = AggregateAdjustedStrategyPnL(strategySymbolTfPnL); var baseResult = BuildResult( nodes, capitalWeights, adjustedSymbolPnL, adjustedStrategyPnL, adjustedPnlTimeline); var walkForwardFolds = await RunTrueWalkForwardAsync( types, selectedMarkets, friction, trustWeightsByType, ct); var result = new PortfolioBacktestResult { StrategyPnL = baseResult.StrategyPnL, SymbolPnL = baseResult.SymbolPnL, CapitalWeights = baseResult.CapitalWeights, PortfolioEquityTimeline = baseResult.PortfolioEquityTimeline, SymbolTimeframePnL = symbolTfPnL, StrategySymbolTimeframePnL = strategySymbolTfPnL, StrategyDiagnostics = strategyDiagnostics, MarketSelectionRejections = combinedRejections, SelectedMarkets = selectedMarkets.Select(x => $"{x.Symbol}::{x.Timeframe}").ToList(), WalkForwardFolds = walkForwardFolds, CioSymbolTimeframeWeights = new Dictionary( cioWeights.ToDictionary( w => $"CIO::{w.Key.Symbol}::{w.Key.Timeframe}", w => w.Value), StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase), MarketAllocationWeights = new Dictionary( marketAllocationWeights.ToDictionary( x => $"{x.Key.Symbol}::{x.Key.Timeframe}", x => x.Value), StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase), CashAllocationWeight = unallocatedCashWeight }; return result; } private Dictionary BuildStrategyTrustWeights( IReadOnlyList strategyTypes) { var raw = new Dictionary(); foreach (var type in strategyTypes) { var strategy = _factory.Create(type); decimal trust = EstimateStrategyTrustScore(type, strategy.Name); raw[type] = System.Math.Max(0m, trust); } decimal totalPositive = raw.Values.Where(x => x > 0m).Sum(); if (totalPositive <= 0m) { decimal equal = strategyTypes.Count == 0 ? 0m : 1m / strategyTypes.Count; return strategyTypes.ToDictionary(x => x, _ => equal); } return raw.ToDictionary( kv => kv.Key, kv => kv.Value <= 0m ? 0m : kv.Value / totalPositive); } private static decimal EstimateStrategyTrustScore(Type type, string strategyName) { decimal prior = GetStrategyTrustPrior(type, strategyName); // Small structural shaping only. // These are intentionally weak so the prior ranking remains the main driver. string typeName = type.Name; string name = strategyName ?? string.Empty; decimal structuralAdjustment = 0m; if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "Trend")) structuralAdjustment += 0.03m; if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "Pullback")) structuralAdjustment -= 0.01m; if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "Rsi")) structuralAdjustment -= 0.01m; return System.Math.Max(0m, prior + structuralAdjustment); } private static decimal GetStrategyTrustPrior(Type type, string strategyName) { string typeName = type.Name; string name = strategyName ?? string.Empty; // REPORT 31 AFTER BASIS FIX: // S05 strongest positive contributor if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "EmaTrendQuantStrategy")) return 1.00m; // S06 still negative, but materially better than S03 if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "RsiSwing")) return 0.30m; // S04 exploratory / weak negative if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "EmaTrendPullback")) return 0.18m; // S03 worst contributor after reconciliation fix if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "EmaRsiQuantStrategy")) return 0.03m; // Keep quarantined if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "AltcoinLeadershipPullback")) return 0.00m; if (ContainsAny(typeName, name, "Diagnostic")) return 0.00m; // Tiny exploratory allocation for unknown future strategies return 0.08m; } private static bool ContainsAny(string typeName, string strategyName, string token) { return typeName.Contains(token, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) || strategyName.Contains(token, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase); } private static WaveBSelectionSnapshot ApplyWaveBSelection( IReadOnlyList rankedSelectedMarkets, Dictionary combinedRejections) { var candidates = new List(); if (rankedSelectedMarkets.Count == 0) return new WaveBSelectionSnapshot(); decimal maxBaseScore = rankedSelectedMarkets .Select(x => SafeDecimal(x.Score)) .DefaultIfEmpty(0m) .Max(); if (maxBaseScore <= 0m) maxBaseScore = 1m; for (int i = 0; i < rankedSelectedMarkets.Count; i++) { var item = rankedSelectedMarkets[i]; MarketKey market = item.Market; decimal baseScore = SafeDecimal(item.Score); decimal normalizedPreTradeScore = baseScore <= 0m ? 0m : baseScore / maxBaseScore; decimal timeframePreferenceScore = market.Timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 1.00m : market.Timeframe.Equals("1d", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 0.80m : 0.55m; decimal liquidityScore = GetLiquidityScore(market.Symbol); decimal leadershipScore = rankedSelectedMarkets.Count == 1 ? 1.00m : 1.00m - (((decimal)i / (rankedSelectedMarkets.Count - 1)) * 0.25m); decimal finalScore = (normalizedPreTradeScore * 0.60m) + (timeframePreferenceScore * 0.25m) + (liquidityScore * 0.15m); finalScore *= leadershipScore; candidates.Add(new WaveBCandidate { Market = market, BasePreTradeScore = baseScore, NormalizedPreTradeScore = normalizedPreTradeScore, TimeframePreferenceScore = timeframePreferenceScore, LiquidityScore = liquidityScore, LeadershipScore = leadershipScore, FinalScore = finalScore }); } var ranked = candidates .OrderByDescending(x => x.FinalScore) .ThenByDescending(x => x.NormalizedPreTradeScore) .ThenBy(x => x.Market.Symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) .ThenBy(x => x.Market.Timeframe, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) .ToList(); var selectedCandidates = new List(); var selectedPerSymbol = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); foreach (var candidate in ranked) { string marketKey = $"{candidate.Market.Symbol}::{candidate.Market.Timeframe}"; if (candidate.FinalScore < WaveBMinScoreThreshold) { combinedRejections[marketKey] = $"WaveBRejected:BelowThreshold(score={candidate.FinalScore:F4},min={WaveBMinScoreThreshold:F2})"; continue; } int currentSymbolCount = selectedPerSymbol.TryGetValue(candidate.Market.Symbol, out int existingCount) ? existingCount : 0; if (currentSymbolCount >= WaveBPerSymbolCap) { combinedRejections[marketKey] = $"WaveBRejected:PerSymbolCap(symbol={candidate.Market.Symbol},cap={WaveBPerSymbolCap})"; continue; } if (selectedCandidates.Count >= WaveBTopNMarkets) { combinedRejections[marketKey] = $"WaveBRejected:TopNOverflow(topN={WaveBTopNMarkets})"; continue; } selectedCandidates.Add(candidate); selectedPerSymbol[candidate.Market.Symbol] = currentSymbolCount + 1; } if (selectedCandidates.Count < WaveBMinMarkets) { foreach (var candidate in ranked) { if (selectedCandidates.Count >= WaveBMinMarkets) break; if (selectedCandidates.Any(x => x.Market.Symbol.Equals(candidate.Market.Symbol, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) && x.Market.Timeframe.Equals(candidate.Market.Timeframe, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))) continue; int currentSymbolCount = selectedPerSymbol.TryGetValue(candidate.Market.Symbol, out int existingCount) ? existingCount : 0; if (currentSymbolCount >= WaveBPerSymbolCap) continue; string marketKey = $"{candidate.Market.Symbol}::{candidate.Market.Timeframe}"; selectedCandidates.Add(candidate); selectedPerSymbol[candidate.Market.Symbol] = currentSymbolCount + 1; if (combinedRejections.ContainsKey(marketKey) && combinedRejections[marketKey].StartsWith("WaveBRejected:", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) { combinedRejections.Remove(marketKey); } } } var allocationWeights = BuildAllocationWeights(selectedCandidates); var cashWeight = System.Math.Max(0m, 1m - allocationWeights.Values.Sum()); return new WaveBSelectionSnapshot { SelectedMarkets = selectedCandidates.Select(x => x.Market).ToList(), AllocationWeights = allocationWeights, CashWeight = cashWeight }; } private static Dictionary BuildAllocationWeights( IReadOnlyList selectedCandidates) { var output = new Dictionary(); if (selectedCandidates.Count == 0) return output; decimal minScore = selectedCandidates.Min(x => x.FinalScore); var shifted = selectedCandidates .Select(x => new { x.Market, Weight = System.Math.Max(0.000001m, x.FinalScore - minScore + 0.000001m) }) .ToList(); decimal shiftedTotal = shifted.Sum(x => x.Weight); if (shiftedTotal <= 0m) return output; var provisional = shifted.ToDictionary( x => x.Market, x => x.Weight / shiftedTotal); var capped = new Dictionary(); decimal overflow = 0m; foreach (var kv in provisional) { if (kv.Value > WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket) { capped[kv.Key] = WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket; overflow += kv.Value - WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket; } else { capped[kv.Key] = kv.Value; } } int redistributionGuard = 0; while (overflow > 0.0000001m && redistributionGuard < 20) { redistributionGuard++; var underCap = capped .Where(x => x.Value < WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket) .ToList(); if (underCap.Count == 0) break; decimal underCapTotal = underCap.Sum(x => x.Value); if (underCapTotal <= 0m) break; decimal distributedThisRound = 0m; foreach (var kv in underCap) { decimal room = WaveBMaxWeightPerMarket - kv.Value; if (room <= 0m) continue; decimal add = overflow * (kv.Value / underCapTotal); if (add > room) add = room; capped[kv.Key] += add; distributedThisRound += add; } if (distributedThisRound <= 0m) break; overflow -= distributedThisRound; } return capped; } private static decimal GetLiquidityScore(string symbol) { if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(symbol)) return 0.50m; if (symbol.StartsWith("BTC", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return 1.00m; if (symbol.StartsWith("ETH", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return 0.95m; if (symbol.StartsWith("SOL", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return 0.90m; if (symbol.StartsWith("BNB", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return 0.88m; if (symbol.StartsWith("XRP", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return 0.85m; if (symbol.StartsWith("ADA", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return 0.82m; if (symbol.StartsWith("DOGE", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return 0.80m; return 0.70m; } private static decimal SafeDecimal(dynamic value) { try { if (value is null) return 0m; return Convert.ToDecimal(value); } catch { return 0m; } } private static Dictionary BuildCompositeMarketScores( IReadOnlyList selectedMarkets, IReadOnlyDictionary rawNetPnlByMarket, IReadOnlyDictionary tradeCountByMarket, IReadOnlyDictionary positiveStrategyHitsByMarket, IReadOnlyDictionary strategyParticipationByMarket, IReadOnlyDictionary leadershipRank) { var scores = new Dictionary(); decimal maxAbsPnl = rawNetPnlByMarket.Count == 0 ? 1m : rawNetPnlByMarket.Values.Select(x => System.Math.Abs(x)).DefaultIfEmpty(1m).Max(); if (maxAbsPnl <= 0m) maxAbsPnl = 1m; int maxTrades = tradeCountByMarket.Count == 0 ? 1 : tradeCountByMarket.Values.DefaultIfEmpty(1).Max(); if (maxTrades <= 0) maxTrades = 1; foreach (var m in selectedMarkets) { decimal pnl = rawNetPnlByMarket.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedPnl) ? resolvedPnl : 0m; int trades = tradeCountByMarket.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedTrades) ? resolvedTrades : 0; int positiveHits = positiveStrategyHitsByMarket.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedPositiveHits) ? resolvedPositiveHits : 0; int participants = strategyParticipationByMarket.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedParticipants) ? resolvedParticipants : 0; int rank = leadershipRank.TryGetValue(m, out var resolvedRank) ? resolvedRank : selectedMarkets.Count; decimal pnlScore = (pnl / maxAbsPnl + 1m) / 2m; decimal activityScore = maxTrades <= 0 ? 0m : (decimal)trades / maxTrades; decimal breadthScore = participants <= 0 ? 0m : (decimal)positiveHits / participants; decimal rankScore = selectedMarkets.Count <= 1 ? 1m : 1m - ((decimal)(rank - 1) / (selectedMarkets.Count - 1)) * 0.35m; decimal timeframeBonus = m.Timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 0.06m : m.Timeframe.Equals("1d", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 0.03m : 0m; decimal score = (pnlScore * 0.50m) + (breadthScore * 0.30m) + (activityScore * 0.20m); score = System.Math.Max(0m, score * rankScore + timeframeBonus); scores[m] = score; } return scores; } private async Task> RunTrueWalkForwardAsync( IReadOnlyList strategyTypes, IReadOnlyList selectedMarkets, FrictionProfile friction, IReadOnlyDictionary trustWeightsByType, CancellationToken ct) { const int foldCount = 3; const decimal trainFraction = 0.70m; var folds = new List(); if (selectedMarkets == null || selectedMarkets.Count == 0) return folds; var baselineMarket = selectedMarkets .OrderBy(x => x.Symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) .ThenBy(x => x.Timeframe, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) .First(); var referenceCandles = _feed.GetCandles(baselineMarket.Symbol, baselineMarket.Timeframe) .OrderBy(c => c.Time) .ToList(); if (referenceCandles.Count < 300) return folds; int total = referenceCandles.Count; int testSize = total / (foldCount + 2); if (testSize < 40) return folds; for (int fold = 1; fold <= foldCount; fold++) { int testEndIndex = total - ((foldCount - fold) * testSize) - 1; int testStartIndex = testEndIndex - testSize + 1; if (testStartIndex <= 0 || testEndIndex >= total) continue; int trainEndIndex = testStartIndex - 1; int trainSize = (int)(trainEndIndex * trainFraction); int trainStartIndex = System.Math.Max(0, trainEndIndex - trainSize + 1); if (trainEndIndex <= trainStartIndex) continue; DateTime trainStartUtc = referenceCandles[trainStartIndex].Time; DateTime trainEndUtc = referenceCandles[trainEndIndex].Time; DateTime testStartUtc = referenceCandles[testStartIndex].Time; DateTime testEndUtc = referenceCandles[testEndIndex].Time; decimal foldPnl = 0m; foreach (var strategyType in strategyTypes) { decimal strategyWeight = trustWeightsByType.TryGetValue(strategyType, out var resolvedWeight) ? resolvedWeight : 0m; if (strategyWeight <= 0m) continue; using var scope = _root.CreateScope(); var strategy = _factory.Create(strategyType); var engine = ActivatorUtilities.CreateInstance( scope.ServiceProvider, strategy); var ledger = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService(); var capital = scope.ServiceProvider.GetRequiredService(); capital.Seed(PortfolioCapital, strategyWeight); foreach (var market in selectedMarkets) { var candles = _feed.GetCandles(market.Symbol, market.Timeframe) .Where(c => c.Time >= testStartUtc && c.Time <= testEndUtc) .OrderBy(c => c.Time) .ToList(); if (candles.Count < 20) continue; var marketWeight = 1m / selectedMarkets.Count; var frictionCost = EstimateFrictionCost( PortfolioCapital * strategyWeight * marketWeight, 0, friction, candles); foreach (var candle in candles) { await engine.OnTickAsync( market.Symbol, candle.Close, candle.Time, ct); } foldPnl += (ledger.TotalPnL * marketWeight) - frictionCost; } } decimal foldStart = PortfolioCapital; decimal foldEnd = PortfolioCapital + foldPnl; decimal foldReturnPct = foldStart <= 0m ? 0m : ((foldEnd - foldStart) / foldStart) * 100m; folds.Add(new WalkForwardFoldSnapshot { FoldNo = fold, TrainStartUtc = trainStartUtc, TrainEndUtc = trainEndUtc, TestStartUtc = testStartUtc, TestEndUtc = testEndUtc, StartEquity = foldStart, EndEquity = foldEnd, ReturnPct = foldReturnPct, TestPoints = System.Math.Max(0, testSize) }); } return folds; } private static PortfolioBacktestResult BuildResult( IReadOnlyList nodes, IReadOnlyDictionary capitalWeights, IReadOnlyDictionary adjustedSymbolPnL, IReadOnlyDictionary adjustedStrategyPnL, IReadOnlyDictionary adjustedPnlTimeline) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(nodes); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(capitalWeights); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(adjustedSymbolPnL); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(adjustedStrategyPnL); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(adjustedPnlTimeline); var equityAggregator = new PortfolioEquityAggregator(); foreach (var kv in adjustedPnlTimeline) equityAggregator.AddPnlDelta(kv.Key, kv.Value); var portfolioEquityTimeline = equityAggregator.BuildFromPnlDeltas(PortfolioCapital); if (portfolioEquityTimeline.Count <= 1) { decimal totalAdjustedPnl = adjustedSymbolPnL.Values.Sum(); DateTime endUtc = DateTime.UtcNow; portfolioEquityTimeline[DateTime.MinValue] = PortfolioCapital; portfolioEquityTimeline[endUtc] = PortfolioCapital + totalAdjustedPnl; } decimal startEquity = PortfolioCapital; decimal endEquity = portfolioEquityTimeline.Count > 0 ? portfolioEquityTimeline.OrderBy(x => x.Key).Last().Value : PortfolioCapital; decimal portfolioDelta = endEquity - startEquity; decimal strategySum = adjustedStrategyPnL.Values.Sum(); decimal symbolSum = adjustedSymbolPnL.Values.Sum(); decimal tolerance = 1.0m; if (Math.Abs(portfolioDelta - strategySum) > tolerance || Math.Abs(portfolioDelta - symbolSum) > tolerance) { throw new InvalidOperationException( "RECONCILIATION FAILURE\n" + $"Portfolio Delta : {portfolioDelta:F2}\n" + $"Strategy Sum : {strategySum:F2}\n" + $"Symbol Sum : {symbolSum:F2}\n" + $"Î” vs Strategy : {(portfolioDelta - strategySum):F2}\n" + $"Î” vs Symbol : {(portfolioDelta - symbolSum):F2}"); } return new PortfolioBacktestResult { StrategyPnL = new Dictionary(adjustedStrategyPnL), SymbolPnL = new Dictionary(adjustedSymbolPnL, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase), CapitalWeights = new Dictionary(capitalWeights), PortfolioEquityTimeline = portfolioEquityTimeline }; } private static void AllocateNetDeltaAcrossClosedTrades( IReadOnlyList closedTrades, decimal netDelta, DateTime fallbackTime, IDictionary adjustedPnlTimeline) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(closedTrades); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(adjustedPnlTimeline); if (netDelta == 0m) return; if (closedTrades.Count == 0) { AddAdjustedPnlPoint(adjustedPnlTimeline, fallbackTime, netDelta); return; } decimal denominator = closedTrades.Sum(t => Math.Abs(t.RealizedPnL)); if (denominator <= 0m) { DateTime time = closedTrades .Select(t => t.ExitTime ?? fallbackTime) .DefaultIfEmpty(fallbackTime) .Max(); AddAdjustedPnlPoint(adjustedPnlTimeline, time, netDelta); return; } decimal allocated = 0m; for (int i = 0; i < closedTrades.Count; i++) { var trade = closedTrades[i]; DateTime time = trade.ExitTime ?? fallbackTime; decimal slice = i == closedTrades.Count - 1 ? netDelta - allocated : netDelta * (Math.Abs(trade.RealizedPnL) / denominator); allocated += slice; AddAdjustedPnlPoint(adjustedPnlTimeline, time, slice); } } private static void AddAdjustedPnlPoint( IDictionary adjustedPnlTimeline, DateTime time, decimal pnlDelta) { if (adjustedPnlTimeline.TryGetValue(time, out var existing)) adjustedPnlTimeline[time] = existing + pnlDelta; else adjustedPnlTimeline[time] = pnlDelta; } private static Dictionary AggregateAdjustedStrategyPnL( IReadOnlyDictionary strategySymbolTimeframePnL) { var output = new Dictionary(); foreach (var kv in strategySymbolTimeframePnL) { int strategyId = ExtractStrategyIdFromStrategySymbolTimeframeKey(kv.Key); if (strategyId <= 0) continue; if (output.ContainsKey(strategyId)) output[strategyId] += kv.Value; else output[strategyId] = kv.Value; } return output; } private static int ExtractStrategyIdFromStrategySymbolTimeframeKey(string key) { if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(key)) return 0; var parts = key.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None); if (parts.Length < 3) return 0; string head = parts[0].Trim(); if (!head.StartsWith("S", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return 0; string numeric = head[1..]; return int.TryParse(numeric, out int id) ? id : 0; } private static Dictionary AggregateAdjustedSymbolPnL( IReadOnlyDictionary symbolTimeframePnL) { var output = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); foreach (var kv in symbolTimeframePnL) { var symbol = ExtractSymbolFromSymbolTimeframeKey(kv.Key); if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(symbol)) continue; if (output.ContainsKey(symbol)) output[symbol] += kv.Value; else output[symbol] = kv.Value; } return output; } private static string ExtractSymbolFromSymbolTimeframeKey(string key) { if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(key)) return string.Empty; var parts = key.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None); if (parts.Length < 2) return string.Empty; return parts[0].Trim(); } private static decimal GetSymbolPnL(TradeLedger ledger, string symbol) { if (ledger.PnLBySymbol.TryGetValue(symbol, out var pnl)) return pnl; return 0m; } private static int GetTradeCount(TradeLedger ledger) { return ledger.TotalTrades; } private static decimal EstimateFrictionCost( decimal positionValue, int tradeCount, FrictionProfile friction, IReadOnlyList candles) { if (tradeCount <= 0 || positionValue <= 0m) return 0m; decimal averagePrice = candles.Count == 0 ? 0m : candles.Average(c => c.Close); if (averagePrice <= 0m) return 0m; decimal grossTurnover = positionValue * tradeCount; decimal stress = friction.StressMultiplier <= 0m ? 1.0m : friction.StressMultiplier; decimal feeRate = BpsToRate(friction.EffectiveFeeBps); decimal slippageRate = BpsToRate(friction.BaseSlippageBps * stress); decimal spreadRate = BpsToRate(friction.BaseSpreadBps * stress); decimal feeCost = grossTurnover * feeRate; decimal slippageCost = grossTurnover * slippageRate; decimal spreadCost = grossTurnover * spreadRate; return feeCost + slippageCost + spreadCost; } private static decimal BpsToRate(decimal bps) { return bps / 10_000m; } private sealed class WaveBCandidate { public required MarketKey Market { get; init; } public decimal BasePreTradeScore { get; init; } public decimal NormalizedPreTradeScore { get; init; } public decimal TimeframePreferenceScore { get; using System.Collections.Generic; using System.Linq; namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio; public sealed class CioDynamicReallocationEngine { private readonly decimal _minWeight; private readonly decimal _maxWeight; private readonly decimal _maxWeightPerSymbol; private readonly int _topK; // Hard block hostile ETH deployment. private static readonly HashSet HardBlockedSymbols = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) { "ETHUSDT" }; // Tighter BTC cap than generic symbol cap. private const decimal BtcHardCap = 0.35m; public CioDynamicReallocationEngine( int topK = 6, decimal minWeight = 0.00m, decimal maxWeight = 0.35m, decimal maxWeightPerSymbol = 0.45m) { _topK = Math.Max(1, topK); _minWeight = Math.Max(0m, minWeight); _maxWeight = Math.Max(_minWeight, Math.Min(1.0m, maxWeight)); _maxWeightPerSymbol = Math.Max(_maxWeight, Math.Min(1.0m, maxWeightPerSymbol)); } public Dictionary ComputeWeights(Dictionary scoreByMarket) { if (scoreByMarket == null || scoreByMarket.Count == 0) return new Dictionary(); // Hard exclusion first. var filtered = scoreByMarket .Where(x => !IsHardBlocked(x.Key)) .ToDictionary(x => x.Key, x => x.Value); if (filtered.Count == 0) return new Dictionary(); var positive = filtered .Where(x => x.Value > 0m) .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value) .ToList(); if (positive.Count == 0) return new Dictionary(); decimal topScore = positive[0].Value; decimal qualityFloor = Math.Max(1m, topScore * 0.15m); var selected = positive .Where(x => x.Value >= qualityFloor) .Take(_topK) .ToList(); if (selected.Count == 0) return new Dictionary(); // Convex spread: leaders get meaningfully higher weight than tail survivors. var raw = selected.ToDictionary( x => x.Key, x => ScoreToConvexWeight(x.Value, topScore)); decimal rawSum = raw.Values.Sum(); if (rawSum <= 0m) return new Dictionary(); var normalized = raw.ToDictionary( x => x.Key, x => x.Value / rawSum); return EnforceConstraintsWithCashFallback(normalized); } private Dictionary EnforceConstraintsWithCashFallback(Dictionary weights) { if (weights == null || weights.Count == 0) return new Dictionary(); var output = weights.ToDictionary(x => x.Key, x => x.Value); // Stage 1: clamp generic market bounds without re-normalizing excess back in. foreach (var key in output.Keys.ToList()) { if (output[key] < _minWeight) output[key] = 0m; else if (output[key] > _maxWeight) output[key] = _maxWeight; } // Stage 2: per-symbol cap with cash fallback ApplyPerSymbolCapWithoutRedistribution(output, _maxWeightPerSymbol); // Stage 3: explicit BTC hard cap with cash fallback ApplySymbolHardCapWithoutRedistribution(output, "BTCUSDT", BtcHardCap); // Final cleanup: keep positive weights only. return output .Where(x => x.Value > 0m) .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value) .ToDictionary(x => x.Key, x => x.Value); } private static decimal ScoreToConvexWeight(decimal score, decimal topScore) { if (score <= 0m || topScore <= 0m) return 0m; decimal ratio = score / topScore; ratio = Math.Max(0m, Math.Min(1m, ratio)); return ratio * ratio; } private static bool IsHardBlocked(MarketKey market) { if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(market.Symbol)) return false; return HardBlockedSymbols.Contains(market.Symbol); } private static void ApplyPerSymbolCapWithoutRedistribution( Dictionary weights, decimal symbolCap) { if (weights.Count == 0) return; var bySymbol = weights .GroupBy(x => x.Key.Symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) .ToList(); foreach (var group in bySymbol) { decimal total = group.Sum(x => x.Value); if (total <= symbolCap) continue; foreach (var item in group) { decimal share = total <= 0m ? 0m : item.Value / total; weights[item.Key] = symbolCap * share; } } } private static void ApplySymbolHardCapWithoutRedistribution( Dictionary weights, string symbol, decimal hardCap) { var symbolItems = weights .Where(x => x.Key.Symbol.Equals(symbol, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) .ToList(); if (symbolItems.Count == 0) return; decimal currentTotal = symbolItems.Sum(x => x.Value); if (currentTotal <= hardCap) return; foreach (var item in symbolItems) { decimal share = currentTotal <= 0m ? 0m : item.Value / currentTotal; weights[item.Key] = hardCap * share; } } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ P o r t f o l i o \ F r i c t i o n P r o f i l e . c s T Y P E : . c s S I Z E : 0 . 6 2 K B L I N E S : 1 8 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio; public sealed record FrictionProfile( decimal MakerFeeBps, decimal TakerFeeBps, decimal BaseSlippageBps, decimal BaseSpreadBps, decimal StressMultiplier = 1.0m, bool PreferMaker = false) { public static FrictionProfile Default => new( MakerFeeBps: 2m, // 0.02% TakerFeeBps: 10m, // 0.10% BaseSlippageBps: 5m, // 0.05% BaseSpreadBps: 3m, // 0.03% StressMultiplier: 1.0m, PreferMaker: false); public decimal EffectiveFeeBps => PreferMaker ? MakerFeeBps : TakerFeeBps; } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio; public sealed class LeadershipRankingService { public IReadOnlyDictionary RankMarkets( ICandleDataFeed feed, IEnumerable symbols, IEnumerable timeframes) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(feed); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(symbols); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(timeframes); var scores = new Dictionary(); foreach (var symbol in symbols) { foreach (var timeframe in timeframes) { var candles = feed.GetCandles(symbol, timeframe) .OrderBy(c => c.Time) .TakeLast(160) .ToList(); if (candles.Count < 80) { scores[new MarketKey(symbol, timeframe)] = decimal.MinValue; continue; } var closes = candles.Select(c => c.Close).ToList(); var ret20 = SafeReturn(closes, 20); var ret60 = SafeReturn(closes, 60); var slope20 = SafeSlope(closes, 20); var vol20 = SafeVol(closes, 20); // Favor strength + trend persistence. // Penalize too-dead / too-flat markets. var score = (ret20 * 0.45m) + (ret60 * 0.35m) + (slope20 * 0.20m) + (vol20 * 0.05m); scores[new MarketKey(symbol, timeframe)] = score; } } return scores; } private static decimal SafeReturn(List closes, int lookback) { if (closes.Count <= lookback) return 0m; var start = closes[^lookback]; var end = closes[^1]; if (start == 0m) return 0m; return (end - start) / start; } private static decimal SafeSlope(List closes, int lookback) { if (closes.Count <= lookback) return 0m; var segment = closes.TakeLast(lookback).ToList(); var first = segment.First(); var last = segment.Last(); if (first == 0m) return 0m; return (last - first) / first / lookback; } private static decimal SafeVol(List closes, int lookback) { if (closes.Count <= lookback + 1) return 0m; var segment = closes.TakeLast(lookback + 1).ToList(); var returns = new List(); for (int i = 1; i < segment.Count; i++) { var prev = segment[i - 1]; var cur = segment[i]; if (prev == 0m) continue; returns.Add(Math.Abs((cur - prev) / prev)); } if (returns.Count == 0) return 0m; return returns.Average(); } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . } public Task RunSelectedAsync( IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies, IReadOnlyList selectedTimeframes, FrictionProfile friction, CancellationToken ct) { return RunSelectedAsync( selectedStrategies, BinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols, selectedTimeframes, friction, ct); } public async Task RunSelectedAsync( IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies, IReadOnlyList selectedSymbols, IReadOnlyList selectedTimeframes, FrictionProfile friction, CancellationToken ct) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedStrategies); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedSymbols); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedTimeframes); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(friction); if (selectedStrategies.Count == 0) throw new InvalidOperationException("No strategies selected."); var result = await _runner.RunAsync( selectedStrategies, selectedSymbols, selectedTimeframes, friction, ct); // PATCH 12: // Canonical post-gating CIO is computed ONCE here, normalized ONCE here, // stored ONCE here, and then read downstream without local recompute or rescaling. var fitnessSvc = new A84StrategyFitnessGatingReportService(); var cfg = new A84StrategyFitnessGatingReportService.FitnessConfig(); var (_, allowedStrategyIds) = fitnessSvc.ComputeFitness(result, cfg); var rawCanonicalCioPostGatingWeights = fitnessSvc.RecomputeCioWeightsWithGating(result, allowedStrategyIds, cfg) ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights = NormalizeCanonicalCioWeights(rawCanonicalCioPostGatingWeights); _alphaRanking.Generate(result); if (result.HasMarketAllocationWeights) { _cioCapital.Generate( result.CapitalWeights, result.MarketAllocationWeights, result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights, result.CashAllocationWeight); } else { _cioCapital.Generate( result.CapitalWeights, runnerMarketAllocationWeights: null, canonicalCioPostGatingWeights: result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights, cashWeight: result.CashAllocationWeight); } _strategyPnl.Generate(result.StrategyPnL); _symbolReport.Generate(result.SymbolPnL); _portfolioEquity.Generate(result.PortfolioEquityTimeline); _portfolioDrawdown.Generate(result.PortfolioEquityTimeline); new SymbolTimeframePnlReportService().Generate(result.SymbolTimeframePnL); new CioWeightsSymbolTimeframeReportService().Generate(result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights); new StrategySymbolTimeframePnlReportService().Generate(result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL); new ReconciliationReportService().Generate(result); // All A84 generation must consume the stored normalized canonical dictionary. new UniversalResearchReportService().GenerateAll( result, DateTime.UtcNow, selectedStrategies); new WalkForwardValidationReportService().GenerateProxyReports( result, DateTime.UtcNow, selectedStrategies); return result; } private static Dictionary NormalizeCanonicalCioWeights( IReadOnlyDictionary source) { var cleaned = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); foreach (var kv in source) { string key = kv.Key?.Trim() ?? string.Empty; decimal value = kv.Value; if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(key)) continue; if (value <= 0m) continue; cleaned[key] = value; } if (cleaned.Count == 0) return cleaned; decimal total = cleaned.Values.Sum(); if (total <= 0m) return new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); var normalized = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); foreach (var kv in cleaned) normalized[kv.Key] = kv.Value / total; return normalized; } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ P o r t f o l i o \ P o r t f o l i o E q u i t y A g g r e g a t o r . c s T Y P E : . c s S I Z E : 1 . 7 6 K B L I N E S : 5 1 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio; public sealed class PortfolioEquityAggregator { private readonly SortedDictionary _timeline = new(); private readonly SortedDictionary _pnlDeltas = new(); public void AddPoint(DateTime time, decimal equity) { if (_timeline.TryGetValue(time, out var existing)) _timeline[time] = existing + equity; else _timeline[time] = equity; } public void AddCurve( IReadOnlyList<(DateTime Time, decimal Value)> points, bool skipMinValueSeed = true) { if (points == null || points.Count == 0) return; foreach (var p in points) { if (skipMinValueSeed && p.Time == DateTime.MinValue) continue; AddPoint(p.Time, p.Value); } } public void AddPnlDelta(DateTime time, decimal pnlDelta) { if (_pnlDeltas.TryGetValue(time, out var existing)) _pnlDeltas[time] = existing + pnlDelta; else _pnlDeltas[time] = pnlDelta; } public Dictionary Build() { return new Dictionary(_timeline); } public Dictionary BuildFromPnlDeltas(decimal startingCapital) { var output = new Dictionary(); decimal runningEquity = startingCapital; output[DateTime.MinValue] = startingCapital; foreach (var kv in _pnlDeltas) { runningEquity += kv.Value; output[kv.Key] = runningEquity; } return output; } public IReadOnlyDictionary Timeline => _timeline; public IReadOnlyDictionary PnlDeltas => _pnlDeltas; } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ P o r t f o l i o \ P o r t f o l i o R i s k B u d g e t E n g i n e . c s T Y P E : . c s S I Z E : 9 . 5 2 K B L I N E S : 2 2 2 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = using TQGA.Domain.Market; namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio; public sealed class PortfolioRiskBudgetEngine { public RiskBudgetDecision Evaluate( string symbol, string timeframe, IReadOnlyList candles, decimal currentPortfolioEquity, decimal currentDrawdownPct, IReadOnlyDictionary openRiskBySymbol, IReadOnlyDictionary openRiskByCluster, decimal currentTotalOpenRiskPct) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(symbol); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(timeframe); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(candles); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(openRiskBySymbol); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(openRiskByCluster); if (candles.Count < 120) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: insufficient candles"); } var last = candles[^1].Close; if (last <= 0m) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: invalid last price"); } var atrPct = EstimateAtrPct(candles); if (atrPct <= 0m) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: invalid ATR"); } var regime = DetectRegime(candles); var regimeMultiplier = regime switch { RiskRegime.HighVolUp => 1.00m, RiskRegime.TrendUp => 0.85m, RiskRegime.Range => 0.35m, RiskRegime.HighVolDown => 0.15m, RiskRegime.TrendDown => 0.10m, _ => 0m }; if (regimeMultiplier <= 0m) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: regime={regime}"); } var cluster = ResolveCluster(symbol); const decimal maxPerSymbolRiskPct = 0.75m; // 0.75% risk budget per symbol const decimal maxPerClusterRiskPct = 1.75m; // 1.75% risk budget per cluster const decimal maxTotalOpenRiskPct = 3.00m; // 3.00% total open portfolio risk var symbolOpen = openRiskBySymbol.TryGetValue(symbol, out var sRisk) ? sRisk : 0m; var clusterOpen = openRiskByCluster.TryGetValue(cluster, out var cRisk) ? cRisk : 0m; if (symbolOpen >= maxPerSymbolRiskPct) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: per-symbol cap reached ({symbolOpen:F2}% >= {maxPerSymbolRiskPct:F2}%)"); } if (clusterOpen >= maxPerClusterRiskPct) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: per-cluster cap reached ({clusterOpen:F2}% >= {maxPerClusterRiskPct:F2}%)"); } if (currentTotalOpenRiskPct >= maxTotalOpenRiskPct) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: total portfolio risk cap reached ({currentTotalOpenRiskPct:F2}% >= {maxTotalOpenRiskPct:F2}%)"); } var drawdownMultiplier = currentDrawdownPct switch { < 5m => 1.00m, < 10m => 0.70m, < 15m => 0.40m, _ => 0m }; if (drawdownMultiplier <= 0m) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, $"REJECT: drawdown throttle active ({currentDrawdownPct:F2}%)"); } // Base risk target per trade decimal baseRiskPct = 0.50m; // 0.50% of portfolio equity // Timeframe preference: your reports keep showing 4h dominance, so allow a small 4h premium. decimal timeframeMultiplier = timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 1.10m : timeframe.Equals("1h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 0.80m : 0.75m; var allowedRiskPct = baseRiskPct * regimeMultiplier * drawdownMultiplier * timeframeMultiplier; var remainingSymbolRoom = Math.Max(0m, maxPerSymbolRiskPct - symbolOpen); var remainingClusterRoom = Math.Max(0m, maxPerClusterRiskPct - clusterOpen); var remainingPortfolioRoom = Math.Max(0m, maxTotalOpenRiskPct - currentTotalOpenRiskPct); allowedRiskPct = Math.Min(allowedRiskPct, remainingSymbolRoom); allowedRiskPct = Math.Min(allowedRiskPct, remainingClusterRoom); allowedRiskPct = Math.Min(allowedRiskPct, remainingPortfolioRoom); if (allowedRiskPct <= 0m) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: no remaining risk budget"); } // ATR sizing: // position value = (portfolio equity * risk%) / ATR% // capped to avoid absurd sizing in very low-vol conditions var rawPositionValue = currentPortfolioEquity * (allowedRiskPct / 100m) / atrPct; var maxPositionValue = currentPortfolioEquity * 0.25m; // hard cap 25% of equity var positionValue = Math.Min(rawPositionValue, maxPositionValue); if (positionValue <= 0m) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: computed position value <= 0"); } var quantity = positionValue / last; if (quantity <= 0m) { return RiskBudgetDecision.Reject(symbol, timeframe, "REJECT: computed quantity <= 0"); } return new RiskBudgetDecision( IsAllowed: true, Symbol: symbol, Timeframe: timeframe, Cluster: cluster, Regime: regime.ToString(), AllowedRiskPct: allowedRiskPct, AtrPct: atrPct, PositionValue: positionValue, Quantity: quantity, Reason: "OK"); } public static decimal EstimateAtrPct(IReadOnlyList candles, int lookback = 14) { if (candles.Count < lookback + 1) return 0m; var slice = candles.TakeLast(lookback).ToList(); decimal trSum = 0m; for (int i = 0; i < slice.Count; i++) { var cur = slice[i]; var prevClose = i == 0 ? cur.Close : slice[i - 1].Close; var tr = Math.Max( cur.High - cur.Low, Math.Max(Math.Abs(cur.High - prevClose), Math.Abs(cur.Low - prevClose))); trSum += tr; } var atr = trSum / lookback; var last = slice[^1].Close; return last <= 0m ? 0m : atr / last; } private static RiskRegime DetectRegime(IReadOnlyList candles) { var closes = candles.Select(c => c.Close).ToList(); if (closes.Count < 120) return RiskRegime.Unknown; var ema21 = closes.TakeLast(21).Average(); var ema50 = closes.TakeLast(50).Average(); var ema120 = closes.TakeLast(120).Average(); var avgAbsRet = AverageAbsReturn(candles.TakeLast(20).ToList()); bool trendUp = ema21 > ema50 && ema50 > ema120; bool trendDown = ema21 < ema50 && ema50 < ema120; bool highVol = avgAbsRet >= 0.012m; if (trendUp && highVol) return RiskRegime.HighVolUp; if (trendUp) return RiskRegime.TrendUp; if (trendDown && highVol) return RiskRegime.HighVolDown; if (trendDown) return RiskRegime.TrendDown; return RiskRegime.Range; } private static decimal AverageAbsReturn(IReadOnlyList candles) { if (candles.Count < 2) return 0m; decimal sum = 0m; int n = 0; for (int i = 1; i < candles.Count; i++) { var prev = candles[i - 1].Close; var cur = candles[i].Close; if (prev == 0m) continue; sum += Math.Abs((cur - prev) / prev); n++; } return n == 0 ? 0m : sum / n; } public static string ResolveCluster(string symbol) { if (new[] { "BTCUSDT", "ETHUSDT", "BNBUSDT", "SOLUSDT", "XRPUSDT", "AVAXUSDT" }.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return "Majors"; if (new[] { "AAVEUSDT", "UNIUSDT", "MKRUSDT", "RUNEUSDT" }.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return "DeFi"; if (new[] { "ICPUSDT", "RNDRUSDT", "FETUSDT", "GRTUSDT" }.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return "AI_Compute"; if (new[] { "ORDIUSDT", "TIAUSDT", "INJUSDT", "SUIUSDT", "SEIUSDT", "JUPUSDT", "WIFUSDT", "ARBUSDT", "OPUSDT" }.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return "Narrative"; return "Other"; } public sealed record RiskBudgetDecision( bool IsAllowed, string Symbol, string Timeframe, string Cluster, string Regime, decimal AllowedRiskPct, decimal AtrPct, decimal PositionValue, decimal Quantity, string Reason) { public static RiskBudgetDecision Reject(string symbol, string timeframe, string reason) => new( IsAllowed: false, Symbol: symbol, Timeframe: timeframe, Cluster: ResolveCluster(symbol), Regime: RiskRegime.Unknown.ToString(), AllowedRiskPct: 0m, AtrPct: 0m, PositionValue: 0m, Quantity: 0m, Reason: reason); } private enum RiskRegime { Unknown = 0, Range = 1, TrendUp = 2, TrendDown = 3, HighVolUp = 4, HighVolDown = 5 } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ P o r t f o l i o \ P r e T r a d e M a r k e t S e l e c t i o n S e r v i c e . c s T Y P E : . c s S I Z E : 6 . 3 3 K B L I N E S : 1 5 7 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = using TQGA.Application.Interfaces; using TQGA.Domain.Market; namespace TQGA.Application.Portfolio; public sealed class PreTradeMarketSelectionService { public SelectionResult SelectMarkets( ICandleDataFeed feed, IReadOnlyList symbols, IReadOnlyList timeframes, int topN = 12) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(feed); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(symbols); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(timeframes); topN = Math.Max(1, topN); var leadership = new LeadershipRankingService() .RankMarkets(feed, symbols, timeframes); var accepted = new List(); var rejected = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); foreach (var symbol in symbols) { foreach (var timeframe in timeframes) { var market = new MarketKey(symbol, timeframe); var candles = feed.GetCandles(symbol, timeframe) .OrderBy(c => c.Time) .TakeLast(220) .ToList(); if (candles.Count < 120) { rejected[$"{symbol}::{timeframe}"] = "REJECT: insufficient history"; continue; } var avgDollarVolume = candles.Average(c => c.Close * c.Volume); if (avgDollarVolume < 2_000_000m) { rejected[$"{symbol}::{timeframe}"] = "REJECT: low liquidity"; continue; } var avgAbsReturn = ComputeAverageAbsoluteReturn(candles); if (avgAbsReturn < 0.006m) { rejected[$"{symbol}::{timeframe}"] = "REJECT: dead / too low volatility"; continue; } var trend = ComputeTrendState(candles); if (trend is not MarketTrendState.TrendUp and not MarketTrendState.HighVolUp) { rejected[$"{symbol}::{timeframe}"] = "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up"; continue; } var maturity = ComputeTrendExtension(candles); if (maturity > 0.18m) { rejected[$"{symbol}::{timeframe}"] = "REJECT: late / overextended trend"; continue; } leadership.TryGetValue(market, out var leadershipScore); decimal timeframeBonus = timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 0.20m : timeframe.Equals("1h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? 0.05m : 0.00m; decimal regimeBonus = trend == MarketTrendState.HighVolUp ? 0.15m : 0.08m; decimal qualityPenalty = maturity * 0.50m; var finalScore = leadershipScore + timeframeBonus + regimeBonus - qualityPenalty; accepted.Add(new SelectedMarket( market, finalScore, avgDollarVolume, avgAbsReturn, trend.ToString(), maturity)); } } var selected = accepted .OrderByDescending(x => x.Score) .Take(topN) .ToList(); var selectedSet = selected .Select(x => x.Market) .ToHashSet(); foreach (var row in accepted.Where(x => !selectedSet.Contains(x.Market))) { rejected[$"{row.Market.Symbol}::{row.Market.Timeframe}"] = $"REJECT: outside top {topN} leadership set"; } return new SelectionResult( selected, rejected); } private static decimal ComputeAverageAbsoluteReturn(IReadOnlyList candles) { if (candles.Count < 2) return 0m; decimal sum = 0m; int n = 0; for (int i = 1; i < candles.Count; i++) { var prev = candles[i - 1].Close; var cur = candles[i].Close; if (prev == 0m) continue; sum += Math.Abs((cur - prev) / prev); n++; } return n == 0 ? 0m : sum / n; } private static MarketTrendState ComputeTrendState(IReadOnlyList candles) { var closes = candles.Select(c => c.Close).ToList(); if (closes.Count < 120) return MarketTrendState.Unknown; var emaFast = closes.TakeLast(21).Average(); var emaMid = closes.TakeLast(50).Average(); var emaSlow = closes.TakeLast(120).Average(); var avgAbsRet = ComputeAverageAbsoluteReturn(candles); bool trendUp = emaFast > emaMid && emaMid > emaSlow; bool trendDown = emaFast < emaMid && emaMid < emaSlow; bool highVol = avgAbsRet >= 0.012m; if (trendUp && highVol) return MarketTrendState.HighVolUp; if (trendUp) return MarketTrendState.TrendUp; if (trendDown && highVol) return MarketTrendState.HighVolDown; if (trendDown) return MarketTrendState.TrendDown; return MarketTrendState.Range; } private static decimal ComputeTrendExtension(IReadOnlyList candles) { var closes = candles.Select(c => c.Close).ToList(); if (closes.Count < 120) return 0m; var last = closes[^1]; var baseline = closes.TakeLast(120).Average(); if (baseline == 0m) return 0m; return Math.Abs((last - baseline) / baseline); } public sealed record SelectionResult( IReadOnlyList SelectedMarkets, IReadOnlyDictionary RejectedMarkets); A p p l i c a t i o n \ R e p o r t i n g \ C o i n P e r f o r m a n c e A n a l y z e r . c s T Y P E : . c s S I Z E : 2 . 6 K B L I N E S : 5 9 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = using TQGA.Domain.Trading; namespace TQGA.Application.Reporting; public sealed class CoinPerformanceAnalyzer { private readonly IReadOnlyList _trades; public CoinPerformanceAnalyzer(IReadOnlyList trades) { _trades = trades.Where(t => t.IsClosed).ToList(); } public string BuildReport() { if (_trades.Count == 0) return "\nNo closed trades → coin analytics unavailable.\n"; var grouped = _trades .GroupBy(t => t.Symbol) .Select(g => { var trades = g.ToList(); var wins = trades.Where(t => t.RealizedPnL > 0).ToList(); var losses = trades.Where(t => t.RealizedPnL < 0).ToList(); var total = trades.Count; var pnl = trades.Sum(t => t.RealizedPnL); var avgWin = wins.Any() ? wins.Average(t => t.RealizedPnL) : 0; var avgLoss = losses.Any() ? losses.Average(t => t.RealizedPnL) : 0; var winRate = total == 0 ? 0 : (decimal)wins.Count / total; var grossWin = wins.Sum(t => t.RealizedPnL); var grossLoss = losses.Sum(t => Math.Abs(t.RealizedPnL)); var pf = grossLoss == 0 ? 0 : grossWin / grossLoss; var expectancy = (winRate * avgWin) - ((1 - winRate) * Math.Abs(avgLoss)); return new { Symbol = g.Key, Trades = total, PnL = pnl, WinRate = winRate * 100, AvgWin = avgWin, AvgLoss = avgLoss, PF = pf, Expectancy = expectancy }; }) .OrderByDescending(x => x.Expectancy) .ToList(); var lines = new List(); lines.Add("\n===== COIN PERFORMANCE MATRIX =====\n"); lines.Add("Symbol | Trades | Win% | PnL | AvgWin | AvgLoss | PF | Expectancy"); lines.Add("-------------------------------------------------------------------"); foreach (var x in grouped) { lines.Add( $"{x.Symbol,-7} | {x.Trades,6} | {x.WinRate,5:F1} | {x.PnL,8:F0} | {x.AvgWin,7:F0} | {x.AvgLoss,8:F0} | {x.PF,4:F2} | {x.Expectancy,10:F2}"); } lines.Add("\nTOP ALPHA MARKET → " + grouped.First().Symbol); lines.Add("WORST MARKET → " + grouped.Last().Symbol); return string.Join("\n", lines); } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . using System.Collections.Generic; using System.IO; using System.Linq; using System.Text; using TQGA.Application.Backtesting; using TQGA.Application.Paths; namespace TQGA.Application.Services; /// /// Alpha decay monitoring using portfolio equity timeline only. /// PATCH 10A: /// Remove A84 ID collisions. /// - CIO Rating exclusively owns A84_03 via A84_03_CIO_RATING /// - Growth Projection exclusively owns A84_04 via A84_04_GROWTH_PROJECTION /// Therefore this service now writes unique non-colliding IDs: /// - A84_07_ALPHA_DECAY_PORTFOLIO /// - A84_08_ALPHA_DECAY_ALERTS /// public sealed class A84AlphaDecayMonitoringReportService { public void Generate(PortfolioBacktestResult result) { Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports); var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine("A84_07 — ALPHA DECAY (PORTFOLIO)"); sb.AppendLine("================================"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine($"Total Points : {pts.Count}"); sb.AppendLine($"Early Half Return : {earlyRet:P2}"); sb.AppendLine($"Late Half Return : {lateRet:P2}"); sb.AppendLine($"Decay Delta : {(lateRet - earlyRet):P2}"); sb.AppendLine(); if (lateRet < earlyRet) sb.AppendLine("Assessment : Alpha decay detected (late period weaker than early period)."); else sb.AppendLine("Assessment : No alpha decay detected by half-split comparison."); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("ROLLING WINDOW DECAY SCAN"); sb.AppendLine("-------------------------"); if (decayScan.Count == 0) { sb.AppendLine("No rolling scan windows were available."); } else { foreach (var row in decayScan.TakeLast(20)) { sb.AppendLine( $"{row.EndUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} UTC | " + $"Window Return: {row.WindowReturn:P2} | " + $"Peak-to-Trough DD: {row.MaxDrawdown:P2}"); } } Write("A84_07_ALPHA_DECAY_PORTFOLIO", sb); var alerts = new StringBuilder(); alerts.AppendLine("A84_08 — ALPHA DECAY (ALERTS)"); alerts.AppendLine("============================="); alerts.AppendLine(); bool decayDetected = lateRet < earlyRet; bool severeDecay = (earlyRet - lateRet) >= 0.10m; bool rollingWeakness = decayScan.Count > 0 && decayScan.Count(x => x.WindowReturn < 0m) >= Math.Max(3, decayScan.Count / 3); alerts.AppendLine($"Decay Detected : {(decayDetected ? "YES" : "NO")}"); alerts.AppendLine($"Severe Decay : {(severeDecay ? "YES" : "NO")}"); alerts.AppendLine($"Rolling Weakness : {(rollingWeakness ? "YES" : "NO")}"); alerts.AppendLine(); alerts.AppendLine("ALERT SUMMARY"); alerts.AppendLine("-------------"); if (!decayDetected && !rollingWeakness) { alerts.AppendLine("No major alpha decay alerts triggered."); } else { if (decayDetected) alerts.AppendLine("- Late-half performance is weaker than early-half performance."); if (severeDecay) alerts.AppendLine("- Decay magnitude is severe by half-split comparison."); if (rollingWeakness) alerts.AppendLine("- Rolling window scan shows repeated recent weakness."); } alerts.AppendLine(); alerts.AppendLine("OPERATIONAL GUIDANCE"); alerts.AppendLine("--------------------"); if (severeDecay || rollingWeakness) { alerts.AppendLine("- Review strategy ranking and top-N execution policy."); alerts.AppendLine("- Check whether edge concentration is too narrow."); alerts.AppendLine("- Investigate whether recent market regime differs from training period."); alerts.AppendLine("- Tighten gating for weak strategies if decay persists."); } else if (decayDetected) { alerts.AppendLine("- Monitor next run closely for continued deterioration."); alerts.AppendLine("- Compare top symbols/timeframes between early and late segments."); } else { alerts.AppendLine("- Continue monitoring; no immediate alpha-decay intervention required."); } Write("A84_08_ALPHA_DECAY_ALERTS", alerts); } private static decimal SegmentReturn(List<(DateTime t, decimal v)> pts) { if (pts == null || pts.Count < 2) return 0m; var start = pts.First().v; var end = pts.Last().v; if (start <= 0m) return 0m; return (end / start) - 1m; } private static List RollingDecayScan( List<(DateTime t, decimal v)> pts, int window) { var output = new List(); if (pts == null || pts.Count < 2 || window < 2 || pts.Count < window) return output; for (int i = window - 1; i < pts.Count; i++) { var slice = pts.Skip(i - window + 1).Take(window).ToList(); var start = slice.First().v; var end = slice.Last().v; decimal ret = 0m; if (start > 0m) ret = (end / start) - 1m; decimal peak = decimal.MinValue; decimal maxDd = 0m; foreach (var p in slice) { if (p.v > peak) peak = p.v; if (peak > 0m) { var dd = (p.v / peak) - 1m; if (dd < maxDd) maxDd = dd; } } output.Add(new DecayWindowRow { EndUtc = slice.Last().t, WindowReturn = ret, MaxDrawdown = maxDd }); } return output; } private static void Write(string name, string title, string body) { var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine(title); sb.AppendLine(new string('=', title.Length)); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine(body); Write(name, sb); } private static void Write(string name, StringBuilder sb) { Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports); File.WriteAllText( Path.Combine( DataPaths.Reports, $"{name}_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"), sb.ToString()); } private sealed class DecayWindowRow { public DateTime EndUtc { get; init; } public decimal WindowReturn { get; init; } public decimal MaxDrawdown { get; init; } } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . } } catch { // best-effort only } var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine("A84_00 — EXECUTIVE SUMMARY"); sb.AppendLine("=========================="); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC): {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}"); sb.AppendLine($"Start Equity : {startEquity:0.00}"); sb.AppendLine($"End Equity : {endEquity:0.00}"); sb.AppendLine($"Total Return : {totalReturnPct:0.00}%"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("POST-GATING CIO SUMMARY"); } } sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("STRATEGIES SELECTED"); sb.AppendLine("-------------------"); if (strategyLines.Count == 0) { sb.AppendLine("NONE"); } else { foreach (var line in strategyLines) sb.AppendLine(line); } sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("TOP STRATEGIES BY PNL"); sb.AppendLine("---------------------"); if (topStrategies.Count == 0) { sb.AppendLine("NO DATA"); } else { foreach (var line in topStrategies) sb.AppendLine(line); } sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("TOP MARKETS BY SYMBOL::TF PNL"); sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------"); if (topMarkets.Count == 0) { sb.AppendLine("NO DATA"); } else { foreach (var line in topMarkets) sb.AppendLine(line); } sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("RECENT GENERATED FILES"); sb.AppendLine("----------------------"); if (recentFiles.Count == 0) { sb.AppendLine("NO RECENT FILES FOUND IN WINDOW"); } else { foreach (var line in recentFiles) sb.AppendLine(line); } File.WriteAllText(outFile, sb.ToString()); } private static string StrategyNameFromSelection( IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies, int strategyId) { var idx = strategyId - 1; if (idx < 0 || idx >= selectedStrategies.Count) return $"Strategy_{strategyId:00}"; return selectedStrategies[idx].Name; } private static string PadRightSafe(string value, int totalWidth) { value ??= string.Empty; if (value.Length == totalWidth) return value; if (value.Length < totalWidth) return value.PadRight(totalWidth); if (totalWidth <= 3) return value[..totalWidth]; return value[..(totalWidth - 3)] + "..."; } private static string FormatUtc(DateTime value) { return value == DateTime.MinValue ? "N/A" : value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"); } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . ""; var w = kv.Value; if (w <= 0) continue; if (key.StartsWith("CIO::", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) key = key.Substring("CIO::".Length); aligned[key] = w; } // Normalize to sum=1 var sum = aligned.Values.Sum(); var slope = EstimateSlopePerStep(slice); var vol = EstimateVolOfStepReturns(slice); var regime = ClassifyPortfolioRegime(slope, vol); labels.Add((pts[i].t, regime, slope, vol)); } // ---- A84_02 transitions ---- var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine("A84_02 — REGIME TRANSITIONS (PORTFOLIO)"); sb.AppendLine("======================================="); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine($"Window : {window} points"); sb.AppendLine($"Points analyzed : {labels.Count}"); prev = x.regime; start = x.t; } } WriteReportFile("A84_02_REGIME_TRANSITIONS", sb.ToString()); // ---- A84_02B stats ---- var sb2 = new StringBuilder(); sb2.AppendLine("A84_02B — REGIME STATS (PORTFOLIO)"); sb2.AppendLine($"{g.Key,-14} {g.Count(),6} {pct,8:P2}"); } sb2.AppendLine(); var last = labels.Last(); sb2.AppendLine($"Current Regime : {last.regime}"); sb2.AppendLine($"Slope (norm) : {last.slope:F6}"); sb2.AppendLine($"Vol (norm) : {last.vol:F6}"); WriteReportFile("A84_02B_REGIME_STATS", sb2.ToString()); } private static decimal EstimateSlopePerStep(List<(DateTime t, decimal v)> slice) { if (slice.Count < 2) return 0m; var first = slice.First().v; var last = slice.Last().v; if (first == 0) return 0m; var n = slice.Count; var ret = (last - first) / first; // total window return return ret / n; // per-step normalized slope } private static decimal EstimateVolOfStepReturns(List<(DateTime t, decimal v)> slice) { if (slice.Count < 3) return 0m; var rets = new List(slice.Count - 1); for (int i = 1; i < slice.Count; i++) { var prev = slice[i - 1].v; var cur = slice[i].v; if (prev == 0) continue; rets.Add((cur - prev) / prev); } if (rets.Count < 2) return 0m; var mean = rets.Average(); var variance = rets.Sum(r => (r - mean) * (r - mean)) / (rets.Count - 1); return SqrtDecimal(variance); } private static string ClassifyPortfolioRegime(decimal slope, decimal vol) { // conservative thresholds if (vol > 0.0125m) { if (slope > 0.0005m) return "HIGHVOL_UP"; if (slope < -0.0005m) return "HIGHVOL_DN"; return "HIGHVOL"; } if (slope > 0.0006m) return "TREND_UP"; if (slope < -0.0006m) return "TREND_DN"; return "RANGE"; } private static decimal SqrtDecimal(decimal x) { if (x <= 0) return 0m; decimal g = (decimal)Math.Sqrt((double)x); for (int i = 0; i < 6; i++) g = (g + x / g) / 2m; return g; } private static void WriteReportText(string name, string title, string body) { var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine(title); sb.AppendLine(new string('=', Math.Max(10, title.Length))); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine(body); WriteReportFile(name, sb.ToString()); } private static void WriteReportFile(string name, string content) { File.WriteAllText( Path.Combine(DataPaths.Reports, $"{name}_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"), content);
