using System.Collections.Generic; using System.IO; using System.Linq; using System.Text; using TQGA.Application.Backtesting; using TQGA.Application.Paths; using TQGA.Application.Portfolio; namespace TQGA.Application.Services; public sealed class A84StrategyFitnessGatingReportService { public sealed class FitnessConfig { public int MinTrades { get; init; } = 30; public decimal MinPnL { get; init; } = 0m; public int MaxStrategiesAllowed { get; init; } = 50; public int TopKMarkets { get; init; } = 20; public decimal MaxWeightPerMarket { get; init; } = 0.10m; public decimal MaxWeightPerSymbol { get; init; } = 0.25m; } public sealed class FitnessRow { public int StrategyId { get; init; } public string StrategyCode { get; init; } = ""; public decimal PnL { get; init; } public int Trades { get; init; } public int Exits { get; init; } public decimal FitnessScore { get; init; } public bool Allowed { get; init; } public string GateReason { get; init; } = ""; } public (Dictionary fitness, HashSet allowedIds) ComputeFitness( PortfolioBacktestResult result, FitnessConfig cfg) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(cfg); var fitness = new Dictionary(); var allowed = new HashSet(); foreach (var kv in result.StrategyPnL.OrderBy(k => k.Key)) { var sid = kv.Key; var pnl = kv.Value; result.StrategyDiagnostics.TryGetValue(sid, out var diag); var trades = diag?.ExecutedEntries ?? 0; var exits = diag?.ExecutedExits ?? 0; const decimal startEquity = 100_000m; var retPct = startEquity <= 0m ? 0m : (pnl / startEquity) * 100m; decimal scoreCore = 0m; if (retPct > 0m && trades > 0) { var logTerm = (decimal)Math.Log(1.0 + (double)(retPct / 100m)); var sqrtTrades = (decimal)Math.Sqrt(trades); scoreCore = logTerm * sqrtTrades; } bool allowedFlag = true; string reason = "OK"; if (trades < cfg.MinTrades) { allowedFlag = false; reason = $"GATED: trades<{cfg.MinTrades}"; } else if (pnl <= cfg.MinPnL) { allowedFlag = false; reason = $"GATED: pnl<= {cfg.MinPnL:0.##}"; } else if (scoreCore <= 0m) { allowedFlag = false; reason = "GATED: fitness<=0"; } var row = new FitnessRow { StrategyId = sid, StrategyCode = $"S{sid:00}", PnL = pnl, Trades = trades, Exits = exits, FitnessScore = scoreCore, Allowed = allowedFlag, GateReason = reason }; fitness[sid] = row; if (allowedFlag) allowed.Add(sid); } if (allowed.Count > cfg.MaxStrategiesAllowed) { allowed = allowed .OrderByDescending(id => fitness[id].FitnessScore) .Take(cfg.MaxStrategiesAllowed) .ToHashSet(); } foreach (var id in fitness.Keys.ToList()) { var r = fitness[id]; if (!allowed.Contains(id) && r.Allowed) { fitness[id] = new FitnessRow { StrategyId = r.StrategyId, StrategyCode = r.StrategyCode, PnL = r.PnL, Trades = r.Trades, Exits = r.Exits, FitnessScore = r.FitnessScore, Allowed = false, GateReason = "GATED: max strategies clamp" }; } } return (fitness, allowed); } public Dictionary RecomputeCioWeightsWithGating( PortfolioBacktestResult result, HashSet allowedStrategyIds, FitnessConfig cfg) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(allowedStrategyIds); ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(cfg); var scoreByMarket = new Dictionary(); foreach (var kv in result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL) { if (!TryParseStrategySymbolTfKey(kv.Key, out var sid, out var symbol, out var tf)) continue; if (!allowedStrategyIds.Contains(sid)) continue; var mk = new MarketKey(symbol, tf); if (!scoreByMarket.ContainsKey(mk)) scoreByMarket[mk] = 0m; scoreByMarket[mk] += kv.Value; } var cio = new CioDynamicReallocationEngine( topK: cfg.TopKMarkets, minWeight: 0.00m, maxWeight: cfg.MaxWeightPerMarket, maxWeightPerSymbol: cfg.MaxWeightPerSymbol); var weights = cio.ComputeWeights(scoreByMarket); return weights.ToDictionary( x => $"CIO::{x.Key.Symbol}::{x.Key.Timeframe}", x => x.Value, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); } public void GenerateAndWrite( PortfolioBacktestResult result, DateTime runUtc, FitnessConfig? cfg = null) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result); cfg ??= new FitnessConfig(); var (fitness, allowed) = ComputeFitness(result, cfg); // PATCH 13C: // A84_05 MUST publish only the exact stored canonical dictionary. // This method is forbidden from using: // - RecomputeCioWeightsWithGating(...) // - MaxWeightPerMarket display logic // - local cleaning / local normalization / local capping var canonicalCio = result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase); var outFile = Path.Combine( DataPaths.Reports, $"A84_05_STRATEGY_FITNESS_{runUtc:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"); var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine("A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS + CIO GATING"); sb.AppendLine("======================================"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC) : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("PUBLISH PATH SIGNATURE"); sb.AppendLine("----------------------"); sb.AppendLine("PATCH_13C_A84_05_CANONICAL_ONLY"); sb.AppendLine("SOURCE = exact result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights"); sb.AppendLine("RECOMPUTE = DISABLED"); sb.AppendLine("LOCAL_CAP = DISABLED"); sb.AppendLine("LOCAL_RESCALING = DISABLED"); sb.AppendLine("LOCAL_CLEANING = DISABLED"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("FITNESS CONFIG (GATING INPUTS ONLY)"); sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------------"); sb.AppendLine($"MinTrades : {cfg.MinTrades}"); sb.AppendLine($"MinPnL : {cfg.MinPnL:0.##}"); sb.AppendLine($"TopKMarkets : {cfg.TopKMarkets}"); sb.AppendLine($"MaxWeightPerMarket : {cfg.MaxWeightPerMarket:P2} (NOT USED FOR A84_05 PUBLISH)"); sb.AppendLine($"MaxWeightPerSymbol : {cfg.MaxWeightPerSymbol:P2} (NOT USED FOR A84_05 PUBLISH)"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("STRATEGY FITNESS TABLE"); sb.AppendLine("----------------------"); sb.AppendLine("Code | PnL | Trades | Exits | Fitness | Allowed | GateReason"); sb.AppendLine("-----+-------------+--------+-------+-----------+---------+---------------------------"); foreach (var row in fitness.Values.OrderByDescending(r => r.FitnessScore)) { sb.AppendLine( $"{row.StrategyCode,-4} | {row.PnL,11:0.00} | {row.Trades,6} | {row.Exits,5} | {row.FitnessScore,9:0.0000} | {(row.Allowed ? "YES" : "NO "),-7} | {row.GateReason}"); } sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine($"Allowed strategies : {allowed.Count} / {fitness.Count}"); sb.AppendLine($"Allowed list : {(allowed.Count == 0 ? "NONE" : string.Join(", ", allowed.OrderBy(x => x).Select(x => $"S{x:00}")))}"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("CANONICAL CIO SNAPSHOT"); sb.AppendLine("----------------------"); sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Count : {canonicalCio.Count}"); sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Sum : {canonicalCio.Values.Sum():P2}"); sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Max : {(canonicalCio.Count == 0 ? 0m : canonicalCio.Values.Max()):P2}"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("CIO WEIGHTS (POST-GATING) TOP 20"); sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------"); if (canonicalCio.Count == 0) { sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Stored canonical CIO weights are empty."); } else { foreach (var w in canonicalCio .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value) .Take(20)) { sb.AppendLine($"{w.Key,-22} W {w.Value:P2}"); } } Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports); File.WriteAllText(outFile, sb.ToString(), Encoding.UTF8); } private static bool TryParseStrategySymbolTfKey( string key, out int strategyId, out string symbol, out string timeframe) { strategyId = 0; symbol = ""; timeframe = ""; var parts = key.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None); if (parts.Length != 3) return false; var s = parts[0].Trim(); if (!s.StartsWith("S", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return false; if (!int.TryParse(s.Substring(1), out strategyId)) return false; symbol = parts[1].Trim(); timeframe = parts[2].Trim(); return !(string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(symbol) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(timeframe)); } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ S e r v i c e s \ A 8 4 S t r a t e g y F i t n e s s R e p o r t S e r v i c e . c s T Y P E : . c s S I Z E : 6 . 9 7 K B L I N E S : 1 6 5 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = using System; using System.Collections.Generic; using System.IO; using System.Linq; using System.Text; using TQGA.Application.Backtesting; using TQGA.Application.Paths; namespace TQGA.Application.Services; /// /// A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS (Institutional heuristic) /// Uses ONLY existing PortfolioBacktestResult fields: /// - StrategyPnL (Dictionary) /// - StrategyDiagnostics (Dictionary) /// /// No dependency on non-existent fields like StrategyTrades. /// public sealed class A84StrategyFitnessReportService { public void Generate(PortfolioBacktestResult result) { Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports); if (result is null) { WriteReportText( "A84_05_STRATEGY_FITNESS", "A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS", "NO DATA: PortfolioBacktestResult is null."); return; } var pnlByStrategy = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary(); var diagByStrategy = result.StrategyDiagnostics ?? new Dictionary(); if (pnlByStrategy.Count == 0 && diagByStrategy.Count == 0) { WriteReportText( "A84_05_STRATEGY_FITNESS", "A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS", "NO DATA: StrategyPnL and StrategyDiagnostics are empty."); return; } // Normalize PnL magnitude so it doesn't dominate everything. var maxAbsPnL = pnlByStrategy.Count == 0 ? 1m : pnlByStrategy.Values.Select(v => Math.Abs(v)).DefaultIfEmpty(1m).Max(); if (maxAbsPnL <= 0) maxAbsPnL = 1m; // Union of strategy IDs from both dicts var ids = pnlByStrategy.Keys .Concat(diagByStrategy.Keys) .Distinct() .OrderBy(x => x) .ToList(); var rows = new List(ids.Count); foreach (var id in ids) { pnlByStrategy.TryGetValue(id, out var pnl); diagByStrategy.TryGetValue(id, out var d); var ticks = d?.TicksProcessed ?? 0; var entryAttempts = d?.EntryAttempts ?? 0; var executedEntries = d?.ExecutedEntries ?? 0; var executedExits = d?.ExecutedExits ?? 0; var signalLong = d?.SignalLong ?? 0; var signalExit = d?.SignalExit ?? 0; // Trades proxy: executed entries var trades = executedEntries; // Execution quality proxies decimal execRate = SafeDiv(executedEntries, entryAttempts); // 0..1 decimal completionRate = SafeDiv(executedExits, Math.Max(1, executedEntries)); // 0..1 decimal churnPenalty = entryAttempts <= 0 ? 0m : SafeDiv(entryAttempts - executedEntries, entryAttempts); // 0..1 decimal discipline = SafeDiv(signalExit, Math.Max(1, signalLong)); // 0..1-ish // PnL scoring decimal pnlScore = Clamp01(Math.Abs(pnl) / maxAbsPnL); decimal directionScore = pnl >= 0 ? 1.0m : 0.0m; decimal activityScore = Clamp01(trades / 5000m); // tune later // Institutional fitness (bounded, deterministic) decimal fitness = (pnlScore * 0.45m) + (directionScore * 0.15m) + (activityScore * 0.20m) + (execRate * 0.10m) + (completionRate * 0.10m) - (churnPenalty * 0.10m); // Hard kill-switch: dead strategy => zero fitness if (trades <= 0) fitness = 0m; rows.Add(new Row( Id: id, PnL: pnl, Ticks: ticks, Trades: trades, EntryAttempts: entryAttempts, ExecutedEntries: executedEntries, ExecutedExits: executedExits, ExecRate: execRate, CompletionRate: completionRate, Discipline: discipline, ChurnPenalty: churnPenalty, Fitness: fitness )); } var ranked = rows .OrderByDescending(r => r.Fitness) .ThenByDescending(r => r.PnL) .ToList(); var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine("A84_05 — STRATEGY FITNESS"); sb.AppendLine("========================="); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("Fitness is a bounded institutional score (0..1) using StrategyPnL + StrategyDiagnostics."); sb.AppendLine("Dead strategies (0 trades) are forced to Fitness 0."); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine($"MaxAbsPnL normalization : {maxAbsPnL:F2}"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("Rank | Strat | Fitness | PnL | Trades | ExecRate | ExitCov | Churn | Discipline"); sb.AppendLine("-----+-------+---------+---------------+--------+----------+---------+--------+-----------"); int rank = 1; foreach (var r in ranked) { var strat = $"S{r.Id:00}"; sb.AppendLine( $"{rank,4} | {strat,-5} | {r.Fitness,7:F3} | {r.PnL,13:F2} | {r.Trades,6} | {r.ExecRate,8:P2} | {r.CompletionRate,7:P2} | {r.ChurnPenalty,6:P2} | {r.Discipline,9:P2}"); rank++; } sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("CIO Action Hint:"); sb.AppendLine("- Only allocate capital to strategies with Fitness >= 0.25 and Trades > 0."); sb.AppendLine("- If Fitness=0, the strategy is inactive (signals not firing or execution path blocked)."); WriteReportFile("A84_05_STRATEGY_FITNESS", sb.ToString()); } private static decimal SafeDiv(int a, int b) => b <= 0 ? 0m : (decimal)a / b; private static decimal Clamp01(decimal x) { if (x < 0m) return 0m; if (x > 1m) return 1m; return x; } private static void WriteReportText(string name, string title, string body) { var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine(title); sb.AppendLine(new string('=', Math.Max(10, title.Length))); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine(body); WriteReportFile(name, sb.ToString()); } private static void WriteReportFile(string name, string content) { var ts = DateTime.UtcNow.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss"); File.WriteAllText( Path.Combine(DataPaths.Reports, $"{name}_{ts}.txt"), content, Encoding.UTF8); } private sealed record Row( int Id, decimal PnL, long Ticks, int Trades, int EntryAttempts, int ExecutedEntries, int ExecutedExits, decimal ExecRate, decimal CompletionRate, decimal Discipline, decimal ChurnPenalty, decimal Fitness); } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . } public void Generate( Dictionary strategyWeights, IReadOnlyDictionary? runnerMarketAllocationWeights, IReadOnlyDictionary? canonicalCioPostGatingWeights, decimal cashWeight) { ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(strategyWeights); var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine("REPORT 06 — CAPITAL ALLOCATION"); sb.AppendLine("================================"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("SECTION A — STRATEGY TRUST WEIGHTS"); foreach (var kv in runnerMarketAllocationWeights.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)) sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key} -> {(kv.Value * 100m):F2}%"); sb.AppendLine($"CASH -> {(cashWeight * 100m):F2}%"); sb.AppendLine(); } else { sb.AppendLine("SECTION B — RUNNER MARKET CAPITAL ALLOCATION"); sb.AppendLine("--------------------------------------------"); sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Runner market allocation weights are empty."); sb.AppendLine($"CASH -> {(cashWeight * 100m):F2}%"); sb.AppendLine(); } if (canonicalCioPostGatingWeights is not null) { sb.AppendLine("SECTION D — POST-GATING CANONICAL CIO ALLOCATION"); sb.AppendLine("------------------------------------------------"); if (canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.Count == 0) { sb.AppendLine("NO DATA: Canonical post-gating CIO weights are empty."); sb.AppendLine(); } else { foreach (var kv in canonicalCioPostGatingWeights.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)) sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key} -> {(kv.Value * 100m):F2}%"); sb.AppendLine(); AppendAllocationMetrics( sb, sectionTitle: "SECTION E — POST-GATING CONCENTRATION RISK", underline: "------------------------------------------", allocationWeights: canonicalCioPostGatingWeights, cashWeight: 0m); } } File.WriteAllText( Path.Combine( DataPaths.Reports, $"REPORT_06_CAPITAL_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"), sb.ToString()); } private static void AppendAllocationMetrics( StringBuilder sb, string sectionTitle, string underline, IReadOnlyDictionary allocationWeights, decimal cashWeight) { sb.AppendLine(sectionTitle); sb.AppendLine(underline); int marketCount = allocationWeights.Count; decimal maxWeight = allocationWeights.Values.DefaultIfEmpty(0m).Max(); decimal minWeight = allocationWeights.Values.DefaultIfEmpty(0m).Min(); decimal totalAllocated = allocationWeights.Values.Sum(); decimal hhi = allocationWeights.Values.Sum(x => x * x); sb.AppendLine($"Markets Allocated: {marketCount}"); sb.AppendLine($"Total Market Allocation: {(totalAllocated * 100m):F2}%"); sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation: {(cashWeight * 100m):F2}%"); sb.AppendLine($"Max Market Weight: {(maxWeight * 100m):F2}%"); sb.AppendLine($"Min Market Weight: {(minWeight * 100m):F2}%"); sb.AppendLine($"HHI Concentration: {hhi:F4}"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("REALISM / RISK FLAGS"); sb.AppendLine("--------------------"); bool wroteWarning = false; if (marketCount == 0) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: No allocated markets."); wroteWarning = true; } if (marketCount == 1) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Single-market allocation. Institutional diversification is absent."); wroteWarning = true; } else if (marketCount <= 3) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Very low diversification. Allocation breadth is thin."); wroteWarning = true; } else if (marketCount < 5) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Low diversification."); wroteWarning = true; } if (maxWeight >= 0.90m) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Extreme concentration. One market dominates almost all capital."); wroteWarning = true; } else if (maxWeight >= 0.80m) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Severe concentration. Max market weight exceeds 80%."); wroteWarning = true; } else if (maxWeight >= 0.60m) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: High concentration. Max market weight exceeds 60%."); wroteWarning = true; } else if (maxWeight > 0.25m) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Elevated concentration. Max market weight exceeds 25%."); wroteWarning = true; } if (hhi >= 0.80m) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: HHI indicates extreme concentration."); wroteWarning = true; } else if (hhi >= 0.50m) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: HHI indicates high concentration."); wroteWarning = true; } if (cashWeight > 0.25m) { sb.AppendLine("WARNING: High idle cash."); wroteWarning = true; } if (!wroteWarning) sb.AppendLine("OK: No major concentration warning under current thresholds."); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR INTERPRETATION"); sb.AppendLine("-----------------------"); if (marketCount == 0) { sb.AppendLine("Capital realism is weak because no allocable markets survived into this allocation set."); } else if (marketCount == 1 || maxWeight >= 0.80m) { sb.AppendLine("Capital realism is weak for institutional use. The system is effectively operating as a single-edge engine."); } else if (marketCount <= 3 || maxWeight >= 0.60m) { sb.AppendLine("Capital realism is moderate-to-weak. Portfolio breadth is limited and concentration risk is material."); } else { sb.AppendLine("Capital realism is acceptable under current simple concentration thresholds."); } sb.AppendLine(); } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . using TQGA.Application.Paths; namespace TQGA.Application.Services; public sealed class FullReportService { // We include both text and CSV outputs in the combined report. // This fixes: "FULL REPORT only contains architecture". private static readonly string[] IncludeExtensions = { ".txt", ".csv" }; public string BuildCombinedReport() { var sb = new StringBuilder(); var files = Directory .EnumerateFiles(DataPaths.Reports, "*.*", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly) .Where(f => IncludeExtensions.Contains(Path.GetExtension(f), StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) .OrderBy(f => Path.GetFileName(f), StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase) .ToList(); return sb.ToString(); } sb.AppendLine("TQGA FULL REPORT"); sb.AppendLine("==============="); sb.AppendLine($"Folder: {DataPaths.Reports}"); sb.AppendLine($"Files: {files.Count}"); sb.AppendLine($"UTC: {DateTime.UtcNow:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}"); sb.AppendLine(); foreach (var file in files) { var name = Path.GetFileName(file); var ext = Path.GetExtension(file); sb.AppendLine($"FILE: {name}"); sb.AppendLine(new string('-', 70)); // CSV: keep it readable but still raw (institutional audit friendly) // TXT: raw sb.AppendLine(File.ReadAllText(file)); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine(new string('=', 70)); sb.AppendLine(); } return sb.ToString(); } public string BuildChatGptSizedReport(int maxChars = 120_000) { var full = BuildCombinedReport(); if (full.Length <= maxChars) return full; // Keep deterministic truncation (no exceptions) return full[..maxChars]; } public string SaveCombinedToFile() { var text = BuildCombinedReport(); var path = Path.Combine( DataPaths.Reports, $"FULL_REPORT_{DateTime.Now:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"); File.WriteAllText(path, text); return path; } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . File.Copy(sourceReportPath, archivedReportPath, overwrite: true); // Web-safe publish content only. string webSafeText = TrimReportForWeb(sourceReportText, WebSafeMaxChars); File.WriteAllText(latestReportPath, webSafeText, Encoding.UTF8); string html = BuildHtmlAuditPage(webSafeText, sourceFileName, timestamp); File.WriteAllText(latestHtmlPath, html, Encoding.UTF8); string reportsIndexHtml = BuildReportsIndexPage(localArchiveRoot); File.WriteAllText(reportsIndexHtmlPath, reportsIndexHtml, Encoding.UTF8); EnsureGitIgnoreRules(gitIgnorePath); // One-time and repeat-safe Git cleanup: // remove any previously tracked large files from index before adding current trimmed files. CleanupGitTrackedLargeFiles(repoRootPath); // Also remove stray heavy files physically from repo root if they exist. CleanupPhysicalLargeFilesFromRepoRoot(repoRootPath); RunGit(repoRootPath, "add ."); RunGit(repoRootPath, $"commit -m \"TQGA auto publish {timestamp}\"", allowNoChanges: true); RunGit(repoRootPath, "push"); SaveRepoPath(repoRootPath); return new GitHubPagesPublishResult { RepoRootPath = repoRootPath, SourceReportPath = sourceReportPath, PublishedLatestTextPath = latestReportPath, PublishedIndexHtmlPath = latestHtmlPath, PublishedArchiveReportPath = archivedReportPath, PublishedReportsIndexPath = reportsIndexHtmlPath, PublicUrl = "https://arifpisonium.github.io/", PublicLatestTextUrl = "https://arifpisonium.github.io/FULL_REPORT_LATEST.txt", PublicReportsIndexUrl = "https://arifpisonium.github.io/reports.html" }; } public string? TryLoadSavedRepoPath() { string path = GetRepoPathConfigPath(); if (!File.Exists(path)) return null; string value = File.ReadAllText(path).Trim(); if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value)) return null; return Directory.Exists(value) ? value : null; } public void SaveRepoPath(string repoRootPath) { ArgumentException.ThrowIfNullOrWhiteSpace(repoRootPath); string path = GetRepoPathConfigPath(); File.WriteAllText(path, repoRootPath.Trim(), Encoding.UTF8); } private static void EnsureGitRepository(string repoRootPath) { string gitFolder = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, ".git"); if (!Directory.Exists(gitFolder)) throw new InvalidOperationException( $"Selected folder is not a Git repository. Missing .git folder at: {repoRootPath}"); } private static string GetRepoPathConfigPath() { string configDir = Path.Combine(AppContext.BaseDirectory, "Config"); Directory.CreateDirectory(configDir); return Path.Combine(configDir, RepoPathConfigFileName); } private static string GetLocalArchiveRoot(string repoRootPath) { string parent = Directory.GetParent(repoRootPath)?.FullName ?? repoRootPath; return Path.Combine(parent, "TQGA_LocalArchives"); } private static void CleanupGitTrackedLargeFiles(string repoRootPath) { RunGit(repoRootPath, "reset HEAD .", allowNoChanges: true); // Remove previously tracked heavy files from Git index only (keep working copy if still present). RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch FULL_REPORT_*.txt", allowNoChanges: true); RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch REPORT_ALL_31_*.txt", allowNoChanges: true); RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm -r --cached --ignore-unmatch reports", allowNoChanges: true); // Re-add current lightweight files later via git add . RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch FULL_REPORT_LATEST.txt", allowNoChanges: true); RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch index.html", allowNoChanges: true); RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch reports.html", allowNoChanges: true); } private static void CleanupPhysicalLargeFilesFromRepoRoot(string repoRootPath) { foreach (string file in Directory.GetFiles(repoRootPath, "FULL_REPORT_*.txt", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)) { TryDeleteFile(file); } foreach (string file in Directory.GetFiles(repoRootPath, "REPORT_ALL_31_*.txt", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)) { TryDeleteFile(file); } string reportsFolder = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, "reports"); if (Directory.Exists(reportsFolder)) { try { Directory.Delete(reportsFolder, recursive: true); } catch { // Keep non-fatal. Git index cleanup above is the critical part. } } } private static void TryDeleteFile(string filePath) { try { if (File.Exists(filePath)) File.Delete(filePath); } catch { // Non-fatal cleanup attempt. } } private static void RunGit(string workingDirectory, string arguments, bool allowNoChanges = false) { string gitExePath = ResolveGitExecutablePath(); using var process = new Process(); process.StartInfo = new ProcessStartInfo { FileName = gitExePath, Arguments = arguments, WorkingDirectory = workingDirectory, RedirectStandardOutput = true, RedirectStandardError = true, UseShellExecute = false, CreateNoWindow = true }; try { process.Start(); } catch (Win32Exception ex) { throw new InvalidOperationException( "Git executable could not be started. " + "Install Git for Windows or add git.exe to PATH. " + $"Resolved git path attempt: {gitExePath}", ex); } string stdOut = process.StandardOutput.ReadToEnd(); string stdErr = process.StandardError.ReadToEnd(); process.WaitForExit(); if (process.ExitCode != 0) { string combined = $"{stdOut}\n{stdErr}".Trim(); if (allowNoChanges && (combined.Contains("nothing to commit", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) || combined.Contains("did not match any files", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) || combined.Contains("fatal: pathspec", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))) { return; } throw new InvalidOperationException( $"Git command failed.\nExecutable: {gitExePath}\nCommand: git {arguments}\n\n{combined}"); } } private static string ResolveGitExecutablePath() { var candidates = new List(); string pathEnv = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("PATH") ?? string.Empty; foreach (string rawPart in pathEnv.Split(';', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries | StringSplitOptions.TrimEntries)) { try { string candidate = Path.Combine(rawPart, "git.exe"); candidates.Add(candidate); } catch { } } candidates.Add(@"C:\Program Files\Git\cmd\git.exe"); candidates.Add(@"C:\Program Files\Git\bin\git.exe"); candidates.Add(@"C:\Program Files (x86)\Git\cmd\git.exe"); candidates.Add(@"C:\Program Files (x86)\Git\bin\git.exe"); string localAppData = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.LocalApplicationData); if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(localAppData)) { candidates.Add(Path.Combine(localAppData, @"Programs\Git\cmd\git.exe")); candidates.Add(Path.Combine(localAppData, @"Programs\Git\bin\git.exe")); } string userProfile = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.UserProfile); if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(userProfile)) { candidates.Add(Path.Combine(userProfile, @"AppData\Local\Programs\Git\cmd\git.exe")); candidates.Add(Path.Combine(userProfile, @"AppData\Local\Programs\Git\bin\git.exe")); } foreach (string candidate in candidates.Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) { if (File.Exists(candidate)) return candidate; } throw new FileNotFoundException( "git.exe was not found. _listener; private CancellationTokenSource? _cts; private Task? _listenLoopTask; private string _siteRoot = string.Empty; private int _port; public int Port => _port; public bool IsRunning => _listener != null && _listener.IsListening; public string Start(string siteRoot, int preferredPort = 8787) { if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(siteRoot)) throw new ArgumentException("Site root is required.", nameof(siteRoot)); if (!Directory.Exists(siteRoot)) throw new DirectoryNotFoundException($"Site root not found: {siteRoot}"); lock (_sync) { if (IsRunning && string.Equals(_siteRoot, siteRoot, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) return BuildBaseUrl(_port); StopInternal(); _siteRoot = siteRoot; _port = FindAvailablePort(preferredPort); _listener = new HttpListener(); _listener.Prefixes.Add($"http://localhost:{_port}/"); _listener.Start(); _cts = new CancellationTokenSource(); _listenLoopTask = Task.Run(() => ListenLoopAsync(_cts.Token)); return BuildBaseUrl(_port); } } public void Stop() { lock (_sync) { StopInternal(); } } private void StopInternal() { try { _cts?.Cancel(); } catch { } try { if (_listener != null && _listener.IsListening) _listener.Stop(); } catch { } try { _listener?.Close(); } catch { } _listener = null; _cts?.Dispose(); _cts = null; _listenLoopTask = null; _siteRoot = string.Empty; _port = 0; } private async Task ListenLoopAsync(CancellationToken ct) { while (!ct.IsCancellationRequested && _listener != null) { HttpListenerContext? context = null; try { context = await _listener.GetContextAsync(); } catch { if (ct.IsCancellationRequested) break; if (_listener == null || !_listener.IsListening) break; } if (context == null) continue; _ = Task.Run(() => HandleRequestAsync(context, ct), ct); } } private async Task HandleRequestAsync(HttpListenerContext context, CancellationToken ct) { try { string relativePath = context.Request.Url?.AbsolutePath ?? "/"; if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(relativePath) || relativePath == "/") relativePath = "/index.html"; relativePath = Uri.UnescapeDataString(relativePath.TrimStart('/')); relativePath = relativePath.Replace('/', Path.DirectorySeparatorChar); string fullPath = Path.GetFullPath(Path.Combine(_siteRoot, relativePath)); string siteRootFull = Path.GetFullPath(_siteRoot); if (!fullPath.StartsWith(siteRootFull, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) { context.Response.StatusCode = 403; await WriteTextAsync(context.Response, "Forbidden", "text/plain", ct); return; } if (Directory.Exists(fullPath)) { string indexPath = Path.Combine(fullPath, "index.html"); if (File.Exists(indexPath)) fullPath = indexPath; } if (!File.Exists(fullPath)) { context.Response.StatusCode = 404; await WriteTextAsync(context.Response, "Not Found", "text/plain", ct); return; } byte[] bytes = await File.ReadAllBytesAsync(fullPath, ct); context.Response.StatusCode = 200; context.Response.ContentType = GetContentType(fullPath); context.Response.ContentLength64 = bytes.LongLength; context.Response.AddHeader("Cache-Control", "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate"); await context.Response.OutputStream.WriteAsync(bytes, 0, bytes.Length, ct); context.Response.OutputStream.Close(); } catch { try { context.Response.StatusCode = 500; await WriteTextAsync(context.Response, "Internal Server Error", "text/plain", ct); } catch { } } } private static async Task WriteTextAsync( HttpListenerResponse response, string text, string contentType, CancellationToken ct) { byte[] bytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(text); response.ContentType = contentType; response.ContentLength64 = bytes.LongLength; await response.OutputStream.WriteAsync(bytes, 0, bytes.Length, ct); response.OutputStream.Close(); } private static int FindAvailablePort(int preferredPort) { for (int port = preferredPort; port < preferredPort + 50; port++) { try { using var listener = new HttpListener(); listener.Prefixes.Add($"http://localhost:{port}/"); listener.Start(); listener.Stop(); return port; } catch { // try next port } } throw new InvalidOperationException("Could not find an available localhost port."); } private static string BuildBaseUrl(int port) { return $"http://localhost:{port}/"; } private static string GetContentType(string path) { string ext = Path.GetExtension(path).ToLowerInvariant(); return ext switch { ".html" => "text/html; charset=utf-8", ".txt" => "text/plain; charset=utf-8", ".csv" => "text/csv; charset=utf-8", ".json" => "application/json; charset=utf-8", ".css" => "text/css; charset=utf-8", ".js" => "application/javascript; charset=utf-8", ".png" => "image/png", ".jpg" or ".jpeg" => "image/jpeg", ".webp" => "image/webp", ".svg" => "image/svg+xml", ".pdf" => "application/pdf", ".zip" => "application/zip", _ => "application/octet-stream" }; } private static void WriteSplitReport( string path, DateTime runUtc, IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies, IReadOnlyList folds) { var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine("WF_01 — TRUE WALK-FORWARD SPLITS"); sb.AppendLine("================================"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC) : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}"); sb.AppendLine($"Strategies Selected : {selectedStrategies.Count}"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("METHOD"); sb.AppendLine("------"); sb.AppendLine("Rule-based walk-forward rerun."); sb.AppendLine("Each fold uses chronological train warmup followed by unseen test window evaluation."); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("FOLDS"); sb.AppendLine("-----"); foreach (var f in folds) { sb.AppendLine( $"Fold {f.FoldNo:00} | TRAIN {f.TrainStartUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} -> {f.TrainEndUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} | TEST {f.TestStartUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} -> {f.TestEndUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} | TestPoints {f.TestPoints}"); } File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString()); } private static void WriteFoldSummaryReport( string path, DateTime runUtc, IReadOnlyList folds) { var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine("WF_02 — TRUE FOLD SUMMARY"); sb.AppendLine("========================="); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC) : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("Fold | Start Equity | End Equity | Return % | Test Points"); sb.AppendLine("-----+--------------+------------+----------+------------"); foreach (var f in folds) { sb.AppendLine( $"{f.FoldNo,4} | {f.StartEquity,12:F2} | {f.EndEquity,10:F2} | {f.ReturnPct,8:F2} | {f.TestPoints,10}"); } var positive = folds.Count(x => x.ReturnPct > 0m); var negative = folds.Count(x => x.ReturnPct < 0m); var stability = folds.Count == 0 ? 0m : (decimal)positive / folds.Count * 100m; sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("SUMMARY"); sb.AppendLine("-------"); sb.AppendLine($"Positive folds : {positive}"); sb.AppendLine($"Negative folds : {negative}"); sb.AppendLine($"Fold stability : {stability:F2}%"); File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString()); } private static void WriteWalkForwardEquityCsv( string path, IReadOnlyList folds) { var lines = new List { "Fold,TrainStartUtc,TrainEndUtc,TestStartUtc,TestEndUtc,StartEquity,EndEquity,ReturnPct,TestPoints" }; File.WriteAllLines(path, lines); } private static void WriteCompactUpload( string path, DateTime runUtc, IReadOnlyList selectedStrategies, IReadOnlyList folds, PortfolioBacktestResult result) { var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("FOLD RETURNS"); sb.AppendLine("------------"); foreach (var f in folds) { sb.AppendLine( $"Fold {f.FoldNo:00} | TestReturn {f.ReturnPct:F2}% | TestPoints {f.TestPoints}"); } var best = folds.OrderByDescending(x => x.ReturnPct).First(); var worst = folds.OrderBy(x => x.ReturnPct).First(); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine("EXTREMES"); sb.AppendLine("--------"); sb.AppendLine($"Best Fold : F{best.FoldNo:00} {best.ReturnPct:F2}%"); sb.AppendLine($"Worst Fold : F{worst.FoldNo:00} {worst.ReturnPct:F2}%"); File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString()); } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . using System.Collections.Generic; using System.Linq; using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection; namespace TQGA.Application.Strategy; /// /// StrategyFactory is the ONLY place responsible for instantiating concrete strategies. /// - Uses ActivatorUtilities so DI can inject dependencies when needed. /// - Also provides discovery of concrete IStrategy types across loaded assemblies. /// public sealed class StrategyFactory { private readonly IServiceProvider _root; public StrategyFactory(IServiceProvider root) { _root = root; } /// /// Create a strategy instance of the provided type using DI. /// The type MUST implement IStrategy and MUST be concrete (not abstract). /// public IStrategy Create(Type strategyType) { if (strategyType is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(strategyType)); if (!typeof(IStrategy).IsAssignableFrom(strategyType)) throw new ArgumentException($"Type '{strategyType.FullName}' does not implement IStrategy."); if (strategyType.IsAbstract || strategyType.IsInterface) throw new ArgumentException($"Type '{strategyType.FullName}' is abstract/interface and cannot be created."); var instance = ActivatorUtilities.CreateInstance(_root, strategyType); if (instance is not IStrategy strategy) throw new InvalidOperationException($"Activator created '{strategyType.FullName}' but it is not IStrategy."); return strategy; } /// /// Discovers all concrete IStrategy types from currently loaded assemblies. /// This avoids Application referencing Infrastructure directly. /// public static IReadOnlyList DiscoverConcreteStrategyTypes() { var types = AppDomain.CurrentDomain .GetAssemblies() .SelectMany(a => { try { return a.GetTypes(); } catch { return Array.Empty(); } }) .Where(t => t is not null && typeof(IStrategy).IsAssignableFrom(t) && !t.IsAbstract && !t.IsInterface) .Distinct() .OrderBy(t => t.Name) .ToList(); return types; } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . using System.Threading; namespace TQGA.Application.Trading; public sealed class TradeDecisionDiagnostics { // ================= INTERNAL COUNTERS ================= private int _ticksProcessed; private int _signalLong; private int _signalShort; private int _signalExit; private int _entryAttempts; private int _executedEntries; private int _executedExits; // ================= PUBLIC READ MODEL ================= public int TicksProcessed => _ticksProcessed; public int SignalLong => _signalLong; public int SignalShort => _signalShort; public int SignalExit => _signalExit; public int EntryAttempts => _entryAttempts; public int ExecutedEntries => _executedEntries; public int ExecutedExits => _executedExits; // ================= ENGINE WRITE API ================= public void OnTickProcessed() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _ticksProcessed); public void OnSignalLong() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _signalLong); public void OnSignalShort() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _signalShort); public void OnSignalExit() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _signalExit); public void OnEntryAttempt() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _entryAttempts); public void OnEntryExecuted() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _executedEntries); public void OnExitExecuted() => Interlocked.Increment(ref _executedExits); public void Reset() { _ticksProcessed = 0; _signalLong = 0; _signalShort = 0; _signalExit = 0; _entryAttempts = 0; _executedEntries = 0; _executedExits = 0; } // ================= REPORT BUILDER ================= public string BuildReport() { var sb = new StringBuilder(); sb.AppendLine($"Signal EXIT : {SignalExit}"); sb.AppendLine(); sb.AppendLine($"Entry attempts : {EntryAttempts}"); sb.AppendLine($"Executed Entries : {ExecutedEntries}"); sb.AppendLine($"Executed Exits : {ExecutedExits}"); return sb.ToString(); } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . _openTrade; public TradingEngine( IStrategy strategy, IOrderExecutor executor, TradeLedger ledger, EquityCurve equity, ICapitalAllocator capital, IRiskManager risk, TradeDecisionDiagnostics diag) { _strategy = strategy; _executor = executor; _ledger = ledger; _equity = equity; _capital = capital; _risk = risk; _diag = diag; } public async Task OnTickAsync( string symbol, decimal price, DateTime time, CancellationToken ct) { // Market sync (executor uses last price as fill in backtests) _executor.UpdateMarketPrice(price); _diag.OnTickProcessed(); // Mark-to-market equity update if (_openTrade != null) { var unrealized = (_openTrade.Side == TradeSide.Buy ? price - _openTrade.EntryPrice : _openTrade.EntryPrice - price) * _openTrade.Quantity; _equity.Update(time, _capital.CurrentEquity + unrealized); } else { _equity.Update(time, _capital.CurrentEquity); } // Strategy decision var context = new StrategyContext( price, time, _openTrade != null, _openTrade?.Quantity ?? 0m); var signal = _strategy.OnTick(context); // ========= ENTRY (LONG) ========= if (signal == TradeSignal.Long) { _diag.OnSignalLong(); if (_openTrade != null) return; if (!_risk.CanContinueTrading()) return; var size = _capital.GetOrderSize(symbol, price); if (size <= 0m) return; if (!_risk.CanEnterPosition(size)) return; _diag.OnEntryAttempt(); await _executor.PlaceMarketOrderAsync( symbol, TradeSide.Buy, size, ct); var fillPrice = _executor.GetFillPrice(); _openTrade = new Trade( symbol, TradeSide.Buy, size, fillPrice, time); _diag.OnEntryExecuted(); return; } // ========= ENTRY (SHORT) ========= if (signal == TradeSignal.Short) { _diag.OnSignalShort(); if (_openTrade != null) return; if (!_risk.CanContinueTrading()) return; var size = _capital.GetOrderSize(symbol, price); if (size <= 0m) return; if (!_risk.CanEnterPosition(size)) return; _diag.OnEntryAttempt(); await _executor.PlaceMarketOrderAsync( symbol, TradeSide.Sell, size, ct); var fillPrice = _executor.GetFillPrice(); _openTrade = new Trade( symbol, TradeSide.Sell, size, fillPrice, time); _diag.OnEntryExecuted(); return; } // ========= EXIT ========= if (signal == TradeSignal.Exit) { _diag.OnSignalExit(); if (_openTrade == null) return; await _executor.ClosePositionAsync(symbol, ct); var fillPrice = _executor.GetFillPrice(); _openTrade.Close(fillPrice, time); // Bookkeeping _ledger.Record(_openTrade); _capital.OnTradeClosed(_openTrade.RealizedPnL); _risk.OnTradeClosed(_openTrade.RealizedPnL); _diag.OnExitExecuted(); _openTrade = null; return; } } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . Parse(string line) { var p = line.Split(','); if (p.Length < 6) return null; return new CandleRow { Time = DateTime.Parse(p[0], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture), Open = p[1], High = p[2], Low = p[3], Close = p[4], Volume = p[5] }; } private static string ToCsv(CandleRow c) { return string.Join(",", c.Time.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"), c.Open, c.High, c.Low, c.Close, c.Volume); } private static void ValidateContinuity(List candles) { var expectedStep = TimeSpan.FromHours(1); for (int i = 1; i < candles.Count; i++) { var diff = candles[i].Time - candles[i - 1].Time; if (diff != expectedStep) { Console.WriteLine( $"⚠ GAP or overlap: {candles[i - 1].Time} → {candles[i].Time} ({diff})"); } } } private sealed class CandleRow { public DateTime Time { get; set; } public string Open { get; set; } = ""; public string High { get; set; } = ""; public string Low { get; set; } = ""; public string Close { get; set; } = ""; public string Volume { get; set; } = ""; } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . DateTime.UtcNow.AddYears(-5); DateTime end = DateTime.UtcNow; var allCandles = new List(); int batch = 0; while (start < end) { await _rateLimiter.WaitAsync(ct); var url = $"https://api.binance.com/api/v3/klines" + $"?symbol={symbol}" + $"&interval={interval}" + $"&startTime={new DateTimeOffset(start).ToUnixTimeMilliseconds()}" + $"&limit=1000"; var data = await RetryPolicy.ExecuteAsync(async () => await _http.GetStringAsync(url, ct)); var json = JsonDocument.Parse(data); if (json.RootElement.GetArrayLength() == 0) break; foreach (var item in json.RootElement.EnumerateArray()) { var line = $"{DateTimeOffset.FromUnixTimeMilliseconds(item[0].GetInt64()).UtcDateTime:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm}," + $"{item[1]}," + $"{item[2]}," + $"{item[3]}," + $"{item[4]}," + $"{item[5]}"; allCandles.Add(line); } // JsonElement does not support the C# Index (^) operator on its indexer, // so compute the last index explicitly. var arrLen = json.RootElement.GetArrayLength(); if (arrLen == 0) break; start = DateTimeOffset .FromUnixTimeMilliseconds( json.RootElement[arrLen - 1][0].GetInt64()) .UtcDateTime .AddHours(1); batch++; progress?.Report(batch); } _writer.AppendOrCreate(symbol, interval, allCandles); } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . Path.Combine(AppContext.BaseDirectory, "MarketData", "Candles") : DataPaths.Candles; } public IEnumerable GetCandles(string symbol, string timeframe) { if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(symbol)) throw new ArgumentException("Symbol is required.", nameof(symbol)); if (!TryDec(parts[3], out var l)) continue; if (!TryDec(parts[4], out var c)) continue; // Volume sometimes missing/blank in some CSVs -> default to 0 decimal v = 0m; _ = TryDec(parts[5], out v); // ✅ Candle is immutable in your Domain: construct via ctor yield return new Candle(t, o, h, l, c, v); return true; } } // ISO time if (DateTime.TryParse( raw, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, DateTimeStyles.AssumeUniversal | DateTimeStyles.AdjustToUniversal, out t)) { t = DateTime.SpecifyKind(t, DateTimeKind.Utc); return true; } t = default; return false; } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . using System.Linq; using TQGA.Application.Strategy; using TQGA.Domain.Indicators; using TQGA.Domain.Trading; namespace TQGA.Infrastructure.Strategies; public sealed class RegimeGatedAltcoinLeadershipPullbackSignal : ISignal { private readonly Ema _ema21 = new(21); private readonly Ema _ema50 = new(50); private readonly Ema _ema200 = new(200); private readonly Rsi _rsi14 = new(14); private readonly Queue _recentCloses = new(); private const int MaxRecent = 80; private decimal _lastPrice; private decimal _previousPrice; private bool _isPrimedForLongReentry; public TradeSignal Evaluate(StrategyContext context) { decimal price = context.Price; _previousPrice = _lastPrice; _lastPrice = price; _ema21.Add(price); _ema50.Add(price); _ema200.Add(price); _rsi14.Update(price); PushPrice(price); if (_recentCloses.Count < 60) return TradeSignal.None; if (!_ema21.IsReady || !_ema50.IsReady || !_ema200.IsReady || !_rsi14.IsReady) return TradeSignal.None; decimal ema21 = _ema21.Value; decimal ema50 = _ema50.Value; decimal ema200 = _ema200.Value; decimal rsi = _rsi14.Value; bool trendAligned = price > ema200 && ema21 > ema50 && ema50 > ema200; bool slopeStrong = ema21 > AverageRecent(10) && ema50 > AverageRecent(20); decimal extensionPctFromEma21 = PercentDistance(price, ema21); decimal extensionPctFromEma50 = PercentDistance(price, ema50); bool tooExtended = extensionPctFromEma21 > 8.50m || extensionPctFromEma50 > 18.00m; if (context.HasOpenPosition) { if (ShouldExitLong(price, ema21, ema50, rsi)) { _isPrimedForLongReentry = false; return TradeSignal.Exit; } return TradeSignal.None; } if (!trendAligned || !slopeStrong || tooExtended) { _isPrimedForLongReentry = false; return TradeSignal.None; } bool controlledPullback = price >= ema50 * 0.985m && price <= ema21 * 1.015m; bool pullbackDepthAcceptable = extensionPctFromEma21 <= 3.75m && price >= ema50 * 0.9925m; bool momentumStillHealthy = rsi >= 48m && rsi <= 68m; bool pullbackStructureHealthy = MinRecent(6) >= ema50 * 0.985m && CountClosesBelow(ema50, 6) <= 2; if (controlledPullback && pullbackDepthAcceptable && momentumStillHealthy && pullbackStructureHealthy) { _isPrimedForLongReentry = true; return TradeSignal.None; } bool bullishResumption = _isPrimedForLongReentry && _previousPrice > 0m && price > _previousPrice && price > ema21 && price > AverageRecent(3) && PercentDistance(price, _previousPrice) >= 0.20m; bool notLateChase = PercentDistance(price, ema21) <= 2.25m; bool localStrengthRecovered = price >= HighestRecent(5) * 0.995m; if (bullishResumption && notLateChase && localStrengthRecovered) { _isPrimedForLongReentry = false; return TradeSignal.Long; } return TradeSignal.None; } private bool ShouldExitLong(decimal price, decimal ema21, decimal ema50, decimal rsi) { bool lostFastTrend = price < ema21 * 0.9925m; bool lostMediumTrend = price < ema50 * 0.9975m; bool momentumFailure = rsi < 43m; bool sharpReversal = _previousPrice > 0m && PercentDistance(_previousPrice, price) >= 3.00m; return lostMediumTrend || (lostFastTrend && momentumFailure) || sharpReversal; } private void PushPrice(decimal price) { _recentCloses.Enqueue(price); while (_recentCloses.Count > MaxRecent) _recentCloses.Dequeue(); } private decimal AverageRecent(int n) { if (_recentCloses.Count == 0) return 0m; return _recentCloses.TakeLast(System.Math.Max(1, n)).Average(); } private decimal HighestRecent(int n) { if (_recentCloses.Count == 0) return 0m; return _recentCloses.TakeLast(System.Math.Max(1, n)).Max(); } private decimal MinRecent(int n) { if (_recentCloses.Count == 0) return 0m; return _recentCloses.TakeLast(System.Math.Max(1, n)).Min(); } private int CountClosesBelow(decimal level, int n) { if (_recentCloses.Count == 0) return 0; return _recentCloses .TakeLast(System.Math.Max(1, n)) .Count(x => x < level); } private static decimal PercentDistance(decimal a, decimal b) { if (b == 0m) return 0m; return System.Math.Abs((a - b) / b) * 100m; } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . } private async Task BuildReportAll31Async(bool copyToClipboard) { string combinedPath = await Task.Run(() => _fullReport.SaveCombinedToFile()); string rawText = await File.ReadAllTextAsync(combinedPath); string formattedText = FormatAuditReportAll31(rawText); string directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(combinedPath) ?? AppContext.BaseDirectory; string report31Path = Path.Combine( directory, $"REPORT_ALL_31_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"); await File.WriteAllTextAsync(report31Path, formattedText); if (copyToClipboard) Clipboard.SetText(formattedText); return report31Path; } private static string FormatAuditReportAll31(string input) { if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input)) return string.Empty; string normalized = input .Replace("\r\n", "\n") .Replace("\r", "\n"); string[] lines = normalized.Split('\n'); var output = new List(lines.Length + 200); bool previousBlank = false; int blankCount = 0; output.Add("TQGA REPORT ALL 31"); output.Add("============================================================"); output.Add($"Generated (UTC): {DateTime.UtcNow:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}"); output.Add("Formatting: Wrapped / normalized / audit-friendly separation"); output.Add(string.Empty); foreach (string rawLine in lines) { string line = rawLine?.TrimEnd() ?? string.Empty; string upper = line.Trim().ToUpperInvariant(); bool isMajorHeader = upper.StartsWith("REPORT ") || upper.StartsWith("A84") || upper.StartsWith("WF ") || upper.StartsWith("WF_") || upper.StartsWith("WALK FORWARD") || upper.StartsWith("FULL REPORT") || upper.StartsWith("TQGA "); if (isMajorHeader && output.Count > 0 && output[^1] != string.Empty) output.Add(string.Empty); if (isMajorHeader) { output.Add("------------------------------------------------------------"); output.Add(line); output.Add("------------------------------------------------------------"); previousBlank = false; blankCount = 0; continue; } if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(line)) { if (!previousBlank || blankCount < 2) { output.Add(string.Empty); blankCount++; } previousBlank = true; continue; } previousBlank = false; blankCount = 0; output.Add(WrapLine(line, 140)); } return string.Join(Environment.NewLine, output); } private static string WrapLine(string text, int maxWidth) { if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(text) || text.Length <= maxWidth) return text; string[] parts = text.Split(' ', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries); var lines = new List(); var current = new System.Text.StringBuilder(); foreach (string part in parts) { if (current.Length == 0) { current.Append(part); continue; } if (current.Length + 1 + part.Length <= maxWidth) { current.Append(' '); current.Append(part); continue; } lines.Add(current.ToString()); current.Clear(); current.Append(part); } if (current.Length > 0) lines.Add(current.ToString()); return string.Join(Environment.NewLine, lines); } private IReadOnlyList GetSelectedStrategyTypes(PortfolioBacktestOrchestrator orchestrator) { if (_strategyList == null || _strategyList.Items.Count == 0) return orchestrator.GetRegisteredStrategies(); List checkedItems = _strategyList.CheckedItems .OfType() .Select(x => x.Type) .ToList(); return checkedItems.Count == 0 ? orchestrator.GetRegisteredStrategies() : checkedItems; } private IReadOnlyList GetSelectedTimeframes() { if (_timeframeList == null || _timeframeList.Items.Count == 0) return AppBinanceUniverse.Timeframes; List checkedItems = _timeframeList.CheckedItems .OfType() .ToList(); return checkedItems.Count == 0 ? AppBinanceUniverse.Timeframes : checkedItems; } private IReadOnlyList GetSelectedSymbols() { if (_coinNameList == null || _coinNameList.Items.Count == 0) return AppBinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols; List checkedItems = _coinNameList.CheckedItems .OfType() .ToList(); return checkedItems.Count == 0 ? AppBinanceUniverse.ActiveSymbols : checkedItems; } private async Task RunSafe(Func action) { Toggle(false); try { await Task.Run(action); MessageBox.Show("DONE"); } catch (Exception ex) { MessageBox.Show(ex.Message); } Toggle(true); } private void Toggle(bool enabled) { if (_btnDownload != null) _btnDownload.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnUpdate != null) _btnUpdate.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnRunResearch != null) _btnRunResearch.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnFullReportSave != null) _btnFullReportSave.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnFullReportClipboard != null) _btnFullReportClipboard.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnPublished != null) _btnPublished.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnReportAll31 != null) _btnReportAll31.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnGitPublished != null) _btnGitPublished.Enabled = enabled; if (_strategyList != null) _strategyList.Enabled = enabled; if (_timeframeList != null) _timeframeList.Enabled = enabled; if (_coinCategoryList != null) _coinCategoryList.Enabled = enabled; if (_coinNameList != null) _coinNameList.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnSelectAll != null) _btnSelectAll.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnSelectNone != null) _btnSelectNone.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnTfAll != null) _btnTfAll.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnTfNone != null) _btnTfNone.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnCatAll != null) _btnCatAll.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnCatNone != null) _btnCatNone.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnCoinAll != null) _btnCoinAll.Enabled = enabled; if (_btnCoinNone != null) _btnCoinNone.Enabled = enabled; } private sealed record StrategyListItem(Type Type) { public override string ToString() => Type.Name; } } = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = F I L E : D : \ D D A T A B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . CURRENT RISK BUDGET ENGINE -------------------------- PortfolioRiskBudgetEngine now decides how much to trust each selected market opportunity. Current dimensions: - ATR sizing - regime multiplier - 4h preference bonus - per-symbol cap - per-cluster cap - total portfolio risk cap - drawdown-based throttling - hard position value cap Purpose: - reduce concentration blowups - smooth fold dispersion - lower over-allocation to unstable markets - improve realism before deeper TradingEngine surgery CURRENT RESEARCH STATUS ----------------------- The platform currently supports: - Strategy backtesting - Symbol PnL attribution - Symbol x Timeframe PnL attribution - Strategy x Symbol x Timeframe attribution - CIO market ranking and capped allocation - Strategy fitness gating - Alpha decay monitoring - Regime classification reports - Executive compact ChatGPT upload summary - Pre-trade market selection - Symbol/category constrained backtest runs - True rule-based walk-forward rerun reporting - Risk-budgeted opportunity scaling KEY CURRENT INSIGHT ------------------- Strongest edge profile remains: - 4h - leadership markets - pullback inside trend - expansion / high-vol regime CURRENT LIMITATION ------------------ Risk budgeting currently scales trust at the portfolio/backtest layer. Full trade-by-trade portfolio budgeting inside TradingEngine remains a later upgrade. NEXT PRIORITIES --------------- 1. TradingEngine trade-level signal ranking + cooldown 2.
